### [40] [Conformal Bootstrap with Duality-Inspired Fusion Rule](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00386)
*Yu Nakayama,Toshiki Onagi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文首次系统地研究了受范畴对称性（非可逆对称性）启发的融合规则的共形场论（CFTs），利用共形自举方法施加了基于Kramers-Wannier对偶的选择规则，并在2到7维空间中推导出最低$\mathbb{Z}_2$-奇标量和偶标量的共形维度界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索具有非可逆对称性结构的CFTs，拓展对强耦合量子场论的理解，特别是传统群对称性无法描述的现象。

Method: 采用共形自举方法，施加由Kramers-Wannier对偶启发的选择规则，数值求解交叉对称性和算符乘积展开的约束，得到共形维度的上下界。

Result: 成功排除了d=3 Ising模型，允许d=2 Ising模型存在；在d=2发现对应于\\mathcal{M}(8,7)极小模型的特征峰；在d=3得到非平庸约束\\Delta_\\sigma \\gtrsim 0.85，对QED$_3$等理论有重要意义。

Conclusion: 证明了非可逆对称性可用于有效约束CFTs，开辟了通过非微扰方法探索受非可逆对称性限制的CFT景观的新途径。

Abstract: We present the first systematic exploration of conformal field theories
(CFTs) possessing fusion rules inspired by categorical (non-invertible)
symmetries, using the conformal bootstrap. Specifically, we impose a selection
rule motivated by Kramers-Wannier duality and derive bounds on the conformal
dimensions $(\Delta_\sigma, \Delta_\epsilon)$ of the lowest-lying
$\mathbb{Z}_2$-odd scalar $\sigma$ and $\mathbb{Z}_2$-even scalar $\epsilon$ in
dimensions $d=2$ through $d=7$. Our bounds correctly allow the $d=2$ Ising
model while excluding the $d=3$ Ising model, demonstrating the effectiveness of
the imposed condition. Furthermore, we observe a distinct feature in $d=2$
corresponding to the $\mathcal{M}(8,7)$ minimal model and find non-trivial
constraints in $d=3$ ($\Delta_\sigma \gtrsim 0.85$), relevant for theories like
QED$_3$. This work opens a new avenue for non-perturbatively probing the vast
landscape of CFTs constrained by non-invertible symmetries.

</details>


### [41] [An algebra for covariant observers in de Sitter space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00622)
*Bin Chen,Jie Xu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在德西特空间中对完整SO(1,d)等距群进行规范化的框架，引入了‘协变观测者’的概念，将观测者的测地线作为动力学实体处理，并在量子化后成为涨落的自由度，形成SO(1,d)的量子参考系。通过构建迹，证明了规范不变可观测量子代数具有II型特征，得到了明确定义的冯·诺依曼熵，并在半经典状态下验证了代数熵与广义熵的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在德西特空间中一致实现引力约束需要规范完整的SO(1,d)对称性，同时需解决多观测者在任意测地线上的相容描述问题。

Method: 引入‘协变观测者’概念，将其测地线视为在等距群下变换的动力学变量；基于类时管定理，以涨落静态斑块内所有自由度生成可观测量代数，并研究其规范不变子代数的结构与类型。

Result: 构造了具有II型特征的平均模交叉积代数，定义了冯·诺依曼熵；在半经典极限下，代数熵与广义熵匹配；推广了局部代数至‘涨落区域’的平均代数。

Abstract: A consistent implementation of the gravitational constraints in de Sitter
space requires gauging the full $SO(1,d)$ isometry group. In this paper, we
develop a framework that enables the gauging of the full de Sitter isometry
while consistently incorporating multiple observers on arbitrary geodesics. We
achieve this by introducing the concept of \textit{covariant observer}, whose
geodesic is a dynamical entity that transforms under the isometry group. Upon
quantization, the geodesic becomes a fluctuating degree of freedom, providing a
quantum reference frame for $SO(1,d)$. Inspired by the timelike tube theorem,
we propose that the algebra of observables is generated by all degrees of
freedom within the fluctuating static patch, including the quantum fields modes
and other observers. The gauge-invariant subalgebra of observables is an
averaged version of the modular crossed product algebra, and we establish its
type II character by constructing a trace. This yields a well-defined von
Neumann entropy. For semiclassical states, by imposing a UV cutoff in QFT and
proposing a quantum generalization of the first law, we demonstrate that the
algebraic and generalized entropies are in match.
  Our work generalizes the notion of a local algebra to that of a
\textit{fluctuating region}, representing an average of algebras over all
possible static patches and configurations of other geodesics. This provides a
complete, covariant, and multi-observer extension of the CLPW construction and
lays the foundation for a fully relational quantum gravitational description of
de Sitter space.

strongly-coupled systems with broken translations. We demonstrate that the

deformed black hole approaches a space like singularity. The anisotropic effect
induced by the axion fields triggers a collapse of the Einstein-Rosen bridge at
the would-be Cauchy horizon, accompanied by a rapid change in the anisotropy of

hole microstates. These invariants exhibit wall-crossing behavior and induce a

identify a generating function for coordinates on the still mysterious quantum
analog of the twistor space.

S-duality, that the generating functions are higher depth mock modular forms.
Moreover, they satisfy a modular completion equation, which fixes their shadow
in terms of other (lower rank) generating functions. We start by bringing about
a significant simplification to these equations and recovering subtle
contributions that were overlooked. Then, we provide (a recipe for) solutions
to these modular completion equations, up to all the holomorphic modular
ambiguities that need to be fixed independently.For this, we use indefinite
generalized theta series and Jacobi-like forms to write the solutions.

</details>


### [50] [Wiggling boundary and corner edge modes in JT gravity with defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01242)
*Kang Liu,Shoupan Liu,Xiao-Mei Kuang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在摆动边界上的Jackiw-Teitelboim（JT）引力中的引力边缘模式（GrEMs）和规范边缘模式（GaEMs），通过引入广义Fefferman-Graham规范扩展边界作用量，并揭示了边缘模式之间的联系及边界自由度的代数结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解在具有摆动边界的JT引力中，引力和规范边缘模式的行为及其相互关系，特别是在存在拓扑缺陷的情况下如何影响边界动力学和物理自由度。

Method: 采用广义Fefferman-Graham规范处理锥形缺陷解，分析边界作用量的红外行为；对虫洞缺陷解，构建具可变质量且受恒定外力作用的场模型，并利用Maurer-Cartan形式将外源矢量信息编码到GaEMs中，结合约束分析与规范分解研究边缘模式。

Result: 发现边界作用量的红外行为由温度和视界位置的局域动力学决定；在特定情况下，虫洞解的边界作用量可映射为受迫振动系统；GrEMs与GaEMs可通过附加约束在角点处关联；角变量构成的“平行四边形”在酉表示下呈现离散性；边界自由度表现为两副本的$\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{R})$代数结构，并识别出规范不变性的拼接条件与可积电荷。

Conclusion: GrEMs和GaEMs在摆动边界条件下通过约束相互关联，边界自由度由拓扑与动力学约束共同决定，其代数结构体现为$\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{R})$对称性，揭示了JT引力中边缘模式的本质特征。

Abstract: We study the gravitational edge modes (GrEMs) and gauge edge modes (GaEMs) in
Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity on a wiggling boundary. The wiggling effect
manifests as a series of spacetime topological and bulk constraints for both
conical and wormhole defect solutions. For the conical defect solution, we
employ the generalized Fefferman-Graham (F-G) gauge to extend the boundary
action, allowing for non-constant temperature and horizon position. We find
that the infrared behavior of this boundary action is determined by the local
dynamics of the temperature and horizon. For the wormhole defect solution, the
boundary action can, in special cases, be described by a field with variable
mass subject to a constant external force. We classify this corner system as a
first-class constrained system influenced by field decomposition, confirming
that the physical degrees of freedom are determined by constraints from the
wiggling boundary information. We find that GrEMs and GaEMs can be linked at
the corners by imposing additional constraints. Additionally, we show that the
``parallelogram'' composed of corner variables exhibits discreteness under a
unitary representation. Finally, we explore that information from extrinsic
vectors can be packaged into the GaEMs via a Maurer-Cartan form, revealing the
boundary degrees of freedom as two copies of the $\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{R})$
algebra. By separating pure gauge transformations, we identify the gluing
condition for gauge invariance and the corresponding integrable charges.

### [51] [Symmetry-Resolved Entanglement Entropy from Heat Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01366)
*Yuan-Chun Jing,Chao Niu,Zhuo-Yu Xian*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于改进热核方法的对称性分辨纠缠熵（SREE）计算框架，解决了传统Sommerfeld公式在含规范场或化学势系统中的局限性，并应用于高斯cMERA态，推导出含化学势的SREE流方程，结果与CFT和全息熵计算一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Sommerfeld公式在处理带电系统时因残差规定不完整和边界条件破坏而失效，需发展适用于含化学势或规范场系统的普适SREE计算方法。

Method: 通过引入符号依赖的相位因子重构热核解析结构，建立全局收敛展开式，并结合Gaussian cMERA态与流函数描述，推导出对称性分辨的纠缠熵流方程。

Result: 得到了适用于任意时空维度的SREE新公式，在μ→0时恢复中性系统结果；在(1+1)维CFT和S1×H^(d-1)全息几何中验证了该框架的正确性。

Conclusion: 该框架统一了中性和带电系统的纠缠熵处理方式，拓展至实空间重整化方法（如cMERA），为研究共形场论、其全息对偶及张量网络表示中的对称性分辨纠缠提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We develop a systematic framework for computing symmetry-resolved
entanglement entropies (SREE) in charged quantum systems based on an improved
heat kernel approach. Although the conventional Sommerfeld formula proves
effective for neutral systems, it encounters limitations when gauge fields or
chemical potentials are introduced due to incomplete residue prescriptions and
violations of asymptotic boundary conditions. By reconstructing the analytic
structure of the heat kernel using a sign-dependent phase factor, we derive a
globally convergent expansion that reconciles discrete residue summations with
continuous spectral decompositions. We further apply this framework to Gaussian
continuous multi-scale entanglement renormalization ansatz (cMERA) states and
show that the entanglement entropy (EE) can be expressed in terms of the cMERA
flow functions. In particular, we obtain a symmetry-resolved entanglement
entropy flow equation in the presence of a chemical potential. This formulation
extends naturally to arbitrary spacetime dimensions and recovers established
results for neutral systems in the mu -> 0 limit. We validate our framework
through two settings: (1) exact agreement with (1+1)-dimensional conformal
field theory (CFT) predictions using twist-operator techniques, and (2)
consistency with holographic entropy calculations on S1 x H^(d-1) geometries.
Our results both unify the treatment of charged and neutral entanglement
entropy and extend this treatment to real-space renormalization frameworks,
providing a robust tool for probing symmetry-resolved entanglement in conformal
field theories, their holographic duals, and cMERA representations.

Result: 证明了八维共形引力中存在唯一的作用量使得爱因斯坦度量为解，并推广至所有偶数维，表明每维都存在唯一的共形不变引力理论（边界项除外）。

### [53] [Emergent Area Operators in the Boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01382)
*Ronak M Soni*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在无体局部自由度的二维和三维情况下固定边界理论中的面积算符，通过定义精确的量子纠错码并展示其具有中心分解，发现由此产生的面积算符在精细尺度上为零，但在粗粒化后出现非零面积算符，其期望值可近似特定非线性子空间态的纠缠熵，且该算符的模糊性与固定面积态的定义模糊性一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过构建精确的量子纠错码，分析其中心分解所导出的面积算符，并研究粗粒化后的行为及其与纠缠熵的关系。

Result: 精细尺度下的面积算符为零；粗粒化后得到非零面积算符，其期望值可近似一类非线性约束态的纠缠熵，且算符的模糊性与固定面积态的定义模糊性相对应。

Conclusion: 面积算符的物理意义依赖于粗粒化过程，其模糊性和非线性约束可解释为半经典性条件，揭示了量子引力中几何量的涌现性质。

Abstract: In some cases in two and three bulk dimensions without bulk local degrees of

central decomposition. However, the area operator that arises from this central
decomposition vanishes. A non-zero area operator, however, emerges after
coarse-graining. The expectation value of this operator approximates the actual
entanglement entropy for a class of states that do not form a linear subspace.
These non-linear constraints can be interpreted as semiclassicality conditions.
The coarse-grained area operator is ambiguous, and this ambiguity can be
matched with that in defining fixed-area states.

### [55] [2D or not 2D: a "holographic dictionary'' for Lowest Landau Levels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01630)
*Gautam Mandal,Ajay Mohan,Rushikesh Suroshe*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在垂直磁场下的二维费米子系统，通过限制在最低朗道能级（LLL），提出了一种将二维量子力学问题映射到一维量子力学的新方法，并建立了精确的1D-2D对应关系，用于描述LLL物理。该对应在大N极限下简化为恒等变换，并给出费米子密度的上限。此外，文章探讨了非对易空间中子区域的纠缠熵行为，发现其既不同于传统二维也不同于一维系统，且不依赖于纠缠区域尺寸的对数项。研究还推广至旋转谐振子陷阱中的二维费米子，表明淬火后动力学可用一维相空间流体力学有效描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于最低朗道能级中x和y之间存在非零的Dirac括号，导致传统的Dirac量子化方法失效，因此需要构建新的框架来正确描述LLL物理。同时，理解非对易空间中的纠缠熵特性以及动力学演化也是推动本研究的重要动机。

Method: 通过构造嵌入在二维量子力学中的一维量子力学体系，建立二维费米子密度与一维Wigner分布之间的精确对应关系，并在大N极限下分析其性质；利用相空间流体力学方法研究淬火后的动力学行为。

Result: 1. 成功构建了一维量子力学模型以准确描述最低朗道能级物理；2. 发现二维费米子密度存在由泡利不相容原理决定的上界；3. 纠缠熵在非对易空间中表现出非传统的标度行为，缺乏对数依赖性；4. 淬火动力学可通过一维相空间流体力学简化计算。

Conclusion: 最低朗道能级系统的物理可以有效地映射到一维量子力学框架下，这种1D-2D对应不仅揭示了非对易几何下的密度约束和纠缠特性，也为强磁场或旋转系统中的动力学提供了简化的理论工具。

Abstract: We consider 2D fermions on a plane with a perpendicular magnetic field,
described by Landau levels. It is wellknown that, semiclassically, restriction
to the lowest Landau levels (LLL) implies two constraints on a 4D phase space,
that transforms the 2D coordinate space (x,y) into a 2D phase space, thanks to
the non-zero Dirac bracket between x and y. A naive application of Dirac's
prescription of quantizing LLL in terms of L2 functions of x (or of y) fails
because the wavefunctions are functions of x and y. We are able, however, to
construct a 1D QM, sitting differently inside the 2D QM, which describes the
LLL physics. The construction includes an exact 1D-2D correspondence between
the fermion density \rho(x,y) and the Wigner distribution of the 1D QM. In a
suitable large N limit, (a) the Wigner distribution is upper bounded by 1,
since a phase space cell can have at most one fermion (Pauli exclusion
principle) and (b) the 1D-2D correspondence becomes an identity transformation.
(a) and (b) imply an upper bound for the fermion density \rho(x,y). We also
explore the entanglement entropy (EE) of subregions of the 2D noncommutative
space. It behaves differently from conventional 2D systems as well as
conventional 1D systems, falling somewhere between the two. The main new
feature of the EE, directly attributable to the noncommutative space, is the
absence of a logarithmic dependence on the size of the entangling region, even
though there is a Fermi surface. In this paper, instead of working directly
with the Landau problem, we consider a more general problem, of 2D fermions in
a rotating harmonic trap, which reduces to the Landau problem in a special
limit. Among other consequences of the emergent 1D physics, we find that
post-quench dynamics of the (generalized) LLL system is computed more simply in
1D terms, which is described by well-developed methods of 2D phase space
hydrodynamics.

</details>

Abstract: We chart the classical moduli space of heterotic strings with broken

### [57] [Localisation with on-shell supersymmetry algebras via the Batalin-Vilkovisky formalism: Localisation as gauge fixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01810)
*Leron Borsten,Dimitri Kanakaris,Hyungrok Kim*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Batalin-Vilkovisky形式，通过引入局部化费米子和规范固定费米子，将局部化与规范固定结合为一个操作。

Abstract: The Batalin-Vilkovisky formalism provides a powerful technique to deal with
gauge and global (super)symmetries that may only hold on shell. We argue that,
since global (super)symmetries and gauge symmetries appear on an equal footing
in the Batalin-Vilkovisky formalism, similarly localisation with respect to
global (super)symmetries appears on an equal footing with gauge fixing of gauge
symmetries; in general, when the gauge-fixing condition is not invariant under
the global symmetries, localisation (with respect to a localising fermion) and
gauge fixing (with respect to a gauge-fixing fermion) combine into a single
operation. Furthermore, this perspective enables supersymmetric localisation
using only on-shell supermultiplets, dispensing with auxiliary fields,
extending an insight first discovered by Losev and Lysov. We provide the first
examples of on-shell localisation for quantum field theories (together with a
companion paper by Arvanitakis).

### [58] [The Double-Copy Root of Hawking Thermality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01832)
*John Joseph M. Carrasco,Yaxi Chen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 通过非阿贝尔规范理论的双拷贝方法，研究坍缩零壳层的霍金辐射谱，发现其在色荷本征值上呈现热谱而非能量热谱，并揭示引力中能量热性与规范理论中电荷热性的对偶关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索霍金辐射在规范/引力对偶下的本质，理解引力热性在对应规范理论中的表现形式。

Method: 利用非阿贝尔杨-米尔斯理论的双拷贝方法，结合大Nc极限和随机矩阵理论中的Wigner半圆律分析色相空间密度。

Result: 辐射谱dN/dλ是普朗克因子与色相空间密度（Wigner半圆）的乘积，表明引力中的能量热性对应于规范理论中色荷的热性。

Conclusion: 霍金辐射在引力中的热性表现为能量热谱，其对偶规范理论中则体现为色荷本征值的热分布，揭示了热性在规范/引力对偶中的深层联系。

Abstract: The Hawking radiation spectrum from a collapsing null shell can be derived
via the double copy of a simpler gauge theory calculation. Analyzing the
non-abelian Yang-Mills root of this process, we demonstrate that the radiation
spectrum is thermal in the color charge eigenvalue $\lambda$, not energy.
Considering the $SU(N_c)$ gauge theory in the large $N_c$ limit, we find the
differential spectrum $dN/ d\lambda$ is a product of the gravitationally
familiar Planck-like factor and the color phase space density, modeled here as
the Wigner semicircle from random matrix theory. This reveals that apparent
energy thermality in gravity is the direct dual of charge thermality in its
underlying non-abelian gauge theory.

</details>

### [59] [Rydberg Single Photon Detection for Probing 0.1-10 meV Dark Matter with BREAD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00145)

Abstract: We introduce a Rydberg-based single photon detector (SPD) for probing dark
matter in the 0.1-10 meV mass range (20 GHz-2 THz). The Rydberg SPD absorbs
photons produced and focused by the BREAD dish antenna and trades them for

Abstract: Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD) is a remarkably rich theory exhibiting numerous
emergent degrees of freedom, from flux tubes to hadrons. Their description in
terms of the underlying quarks and gluons of the QCD Lagrangian remains a

probe these phenomena experimentally: high energy partons produced from the QCD
vacuum excite these emergent degrees, imprinting their dynamics in correlations
in asymptotic energy flux. Decoding these correlations requires measurements
with exceptional angular resolution, beyond that achieved in previous
measurements. Recent progress has enabled precision calculations of energy flux
on charged particles alone, allowing data-theory comparisons for measurements
using high resolution tracking detectors. In this Letter, we resurrect
thirty-year-old data from the ALEPH tracker, and perform a high angular
resolution measurement of the two-point correlation of energy flux, probing QCD
over three orders of magnitude in scale in a single measurement. Our
measurement unveils for the first time the full spectrum of the correlator,
including light-ray quasi-particle states, flux-tube excitations, and their
transitions into confined hadrons. We compare our measurement with record
precision theoretical predictions, achieving percent level agreement, and
revealing interesting new phenomena in the confinement transitions. More
broadly, we highlight the immense potential of this newly unlocked archival
data set, the so called "recycling frontier", and emphasize synergies with
ongoing and future collider experiments.

Abstract: We introduce a phenomenological modification of the MIT bag model equation of

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有核模型（如NuWro、GiBUU、RMF+Achilles）无法同时描述JSNS²实验中缺失能谱的谱宽和高能尾，反映出在结合能、2p-2h激发和末态相互作用处理上的不足，需构建更准确的经验模型。

Result: 新模型在6个自由度下将χ²从现有模型的35.5–176.8大幅降低至8.0，成功再现了缺失能谱的整体形状，量化了s壳层的不对称展宽，同时保持p壳层窄化的准弹性响应。

$^{12}$C at 235.5~MeV have compared the measured missing-energy spectrum with
several nuclear models, including \textsc{NuWro}, \textsc{GiBUU}, and
RMF+Achilles. While these models reproduce the overall peak position, their
respective $\chi^2$ values of $35.5$, $176.8$, and $58.1$ indicate that none
can simultaneously describe the spectral width and the high-energy tail,
reflecting limitations in the treatment of binding energy,
two-particle--two-hole (2p--2h) excitations, and final-state interactions
(FSI). To address these discrepancies, we introduce an empirical yet physically
motivated representation of the spectrum based on two exponentially modified
Gaussian (ex-Gaussian) components for p- and s-shell knockout and a generalized
power--exponential continuum term describing multinucleon and FSI-induced
strength. The fit reproduces the JSNS$^2$ data within the fitted energy range
with $\chi^2=8.0$ for 6 degrees of freedom. yielding parameters that quantify
asymmetric broadening of the s-shell while preserving a narrow quasielastic
p-shell response. This compact model demonstrates that a minimal empirical
framework can capture key features of the nuclear response and provides a
useful reference for phenomenological comparisons and future studies of
quasielastic and 2p--2h dynamics in the few-hundred-MeV regime.

*Krishna Tewary,Sanjoy Biswas,Shivam Verma*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了标准模型的门户矢量类轻子（pVLL）扩展，在未来μ子对撞机上探讨其对Higgs与矢量玻色子（hV，V为Z玻色子或暗光子）关联产生过程的影响。结果表明，μ⁺μ⁻ → hγ_d 的产率可显著增强，并可能超过hZ产率1-100倍，成为探测Higgs物理和新物理效应的重要通道。同时，该过程可用于约束暗光子质量与暗规范耦合。在b̄b+缺失能量末态的分析中，可在一定参数下对m_γ_d 达到75 GeV的2σ排除限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索标准模型之外的新物理，特别是通过门户矢量类轻子模型连接可见世界与暗物质 sector，并利用未来μ子对撞机高精度探测Higgs与矢量玻色子的关联产生过程。

Method: 基于pVLL模型扩展标准模型，计算μ⁺μ⁻ → hZ 和 μ⁺μ⁻ → hγ_d 的产生截面，并在满足微扰幺正性的参数空间内分析信号产率；针对b̄b + 缺失能量末态开展详细对撞机模拟与灵敏度分析。

Result: μ⁺μ⁻ → hZ 产率接近标准模型预测，而 μ⁺μ⁻ → hγ_d 可显著增强，最高可达hZ产率的100倍；在3 TeV μ子对撞机、1 ab⁻¹积分亮度下，可对m_γ_d 达到75 GeV的2σ排除限（特定参数下）。

Conclusion: hγ_d 关联产生是探测pVLL模型及暗光子参数的极佳探针，具有强非解耦效应，在未来μ子对撞机上极具发现潜力。

Abstract: We have explored a portal vector-like lepton (pVLL) extension of the Standard
Model (SM) and studied its implications for Higgs and vector-boson associated
production ($hV$, with $~V = Z$-boson or dark photon) at a future muon collider
facility. We show that while the $~\mu^+ \mu^- \to hZ~$ production rate remains
close to its SM prediction in a wide range of parameter space, the rate for
$~\mu^+ \mu^- \to h\gamma_d~$ can be substantially enhanced owing to the
non-decoupling nature of the interaction involving the heavy lepton, the muon
and the dark photon. We demonstrate that the $h\gamma_d$ production rate can
exceed the corresponding $hZ$ rate by a factor of $1$-$100$ within the
perturbative unitarity limit, making it a promising channel for probing Higgs
interactions and potential new physics effects.
  Furthermore, this process can also be used to constrain the dark photon mass
($m_{\gamma_d}$) and/or the dark gauge coupling ($g_d$) within the pVLL
framework. We perform a detailed collider analysis of the $h\gamma_d$ process
in the $b\bar{b}~+$ missing energy final state. A $2\sigma$ exclusion limit for
$m_{\gamma_d}$ up to $75$ GeV is obtained assuming $~g_d=0.05$,
$~\sin\theta_L=4\times10^{-5}$, $~\sin\theta_s=0.05$, and heavy lepton mass
$\gtrsim 2$ TeV at a $3$ TeV muon collider with an integrated luminosity of $1$
ab$^{-1}$.

</details>

### [76] [U-spin symmetry energy and hyperon puzzle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01325)
*Hao-Song You,Ting-Lan Yu,Cheng-Jun Xia,Ren-Xin Xu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 提出超子物质的U-对称能$E_\mathrm{U}(n_\mathrm{b})$，用于描述包含超子时结合能的变化，并利用贝叶斯推断方法确定其值。结果表明，$E_\mathrm{U}$远小于核对称能$E_\mathrm{sym}$，意味着核子-超子吸引力弱于质子-中子吸引力，导致高密度下$\Lambda$超子势显著增大并呈排斥性，多数情况下$\Lambda$超子在中子星中不出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于SU(3)味对称性分解为子群的思想，类比核物质中的同位旋对称能，建立超子物质中的U-对称能以系统描述超子引入后结合能的变化规律，并探究超子在中子星高密环境下的行为。

Method: 通过(u,d)同位旋双态或(d,s)U-旋双态构建SU(2)$_I\times$U(1)$_Y$或SU(2)$_U\times$U(1)$_Q$子群，定义U-对称能$E_\mathrm{U}(n_\mathrm{b})$；结合核物理与天体观测的最新约束，采用贝叶斯推断方法确定$E_\mathrm{U}(n_\mathrm{b})$及其对$\Lambda$超子势的影响。

Result: $E_\mathrm{U}(n_\mathrm{b})$明显小于$E_\mathrm{sym}(n_\mathrm{b})$，表明核子-超子间吸引力弱于质子-中子间；高密度下$\Lambda$超子势显著上升并趋于排斥，超过80%概率下$\Lambda$超子不在中子星中出现；若出现，其阈值密度$n_\mathrm{b}^\Lambda > \sim0.8\,\mathrm{fm}^{-3}$，对应中子星质量大于1.7$M_\odot$。

Conclusion: U-对称能框架有效刻画了超子物质中结合能的变化，揭示了$\Lambda$超子在高密条件下难以形成的趋势，支持中子星内部可能不含或仅在极高密度下含少量$\Lambda$超子的观点。

Abstract: By combining the (u,d) I-spin doublets or (d,s) U-spin doublets, the SU(3)
flavor symmetry of light quarks can be decomposed into SU(2)$_I\times$U(1)$_Y$
or SU(2)$_U\times$U(1)$_Q$ subgroups, which have been widely adopted to
categorize hadrons and their decay properties. The I-spin counterpart for the
interactions among nucleons has been extensively investigated, i.e., the
nuclear symmetry energy $E_\mathrm{sym}(n_\mathrm{b})$, which characterizes the
variation of binding energy as the neutron to proton ratio in a nuclear system.
In this work, we propose U-spin symmetry energy $E_\mathrm{U}(n_\mathrm{b})$
for hyperonic matter to characterize the variation of the binding energy with
the inclusion of hyperons. In particular, being the lightest hyperon, $\Lambda$
hyperons are included in dense matter, where the U-spin symmetry energy
$E_\mathrm{U}(n_\mathrm{b})$ is fixed according to state-of-the-art constraints
from nuclear physics and astrophysical observations using Bayesian inference
approach. It is found that $E_\mathrm{U}(n_\mathrm{b})$ is much smaller than
that of $E_\mathrm{sym}(n_\mathrm{b})$, indicating much stronger proton-neutron
attraction than that of nucleon-hyperon pairs. Consequently, $\Lambda$ hyperon
potential increases significantly and becomes repulsive at large density, where
there is more than 80\% probability that $\Lambda$ hyperons do not emerge in
neutron stars. For those undergoing emergence within neutron stars, the onset
density of $\Lambda$ hyperons $n_\mathrm{b}^\Lambda$ is typically larger than
$\sim$0.8 fm$^{-3}$, corresponding to neutron stars more massive than 1.7
$M_\odot$.

*Diganta Das,Mihika Sanghi,Sourav*

TL;DR: 本文研究了暴胀后重加热时期原初随机引力波的产生机制，特别是暴胀子衰变为自旋3/2粒子并伴随引力子发射的过程，并通过数值模拟计算了引力波谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探测原初引力波可为暴胀提供直接证据，并揭示早期宇宙的动力学信息。重加热阶段暴胀子相干振荡可能激发引力波，但其与不同自旋粒子的相互作用尚需深入研究。

Method: 假设势能在极小值附近呈多项式形式V(φ)~φ^k（k≥2），将暴胀子视为相干振荡的经典场，计算其衰变为一对自旋3/2粒子并辐射引力子的过程，数值模拟重加热动力学并计算随机引力波谱。

Result: 成功计算出自旋3/2粒子产生下的随机引力波谱，发现该谱特征可反映暴胀时期的微观物理过程。

Conclusion: 引力波谱不仅是暴胀的探针，还可用于约束暴胀模型中的粒子物理机制，为理解早期宇宙提供新途径。

Abstract: The detection of primordial gravitational waves would offer a direct evidence
of inflation and valuable insights into the dynamics of the early universe.
During post-inflation reheating period, when the inflaton coherently oscillates
at the bottom of its potential, primordial stochastic gravitational waves may
be sourced by its perturbative decay into particles of different spins.
Assuming the behavior of the potential near the minimum as a polynomial
$V(\phi)\sim \phi^k$, where $k\ge 2$, and treating the inflaton as coherently
oscillating classical field, we calculate the decay of inflaton into a pair of
spin $3/2$ particles accompanied by graviton emission. We numerically study the
reheating dynamics and calculate the stochastic gravitational wave spectra. Our
analysis shows that the gravitational wave spectra can offer insights into the
microscopic physics during inflation.

</details>


### [79] [Direct detection of solar chameleons with electron recoil data from XENONnT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01655)
*Guan-Wen Yuan,Anne-Christine Davis,Maurizio Giannotti,Sunny Vagnozzi,Luca Visinelli,Julia K. Vogel*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新评估了太阳变色龙粒子的直接探测前景，考虑了其产生的新模型和XENONnT实验数据。研究发现，电子和离子电场中的Primakoff效应主导了电子反冲事件率，信号由有效耦合β_eff决定。利用XENONnT数据，得到了对逆幂律变色龙模型的普适上限log₁₀β_eff < -6.9，该结果独立于物质耦合参数，适用于广泛的变色龙模型。研究表明现有暗物质实验可有效探测屏蔽暗能量模型的参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变色龙粒子是屏蔽暗能量模型中的候选者，但其产生机制和探测前景尚不明确。先前研究仅考虑磁转换过程，低估了信号强度。需要结合新的产生机制模型和最新实验数据，重新评估其可探测性。

Method: 通过计算电子和离子电场中Primakoff过程对变色龙粒子产生的贡献，结合XENONnT实验的电子反冲数据，分析信号事件率并提取有效耦合β_eff的约束。推导出适用于一般逆幂律势的普适限制，且不依赖于具体的物质耦合参数。

Result: Primakoff过程在电场中的贡献主导电子反冲率，显著增强信号；基于XENONnT数据得出log₁₀β_eff < -6.9的上限；该限制适用于所有逆幂律变色龙模型，而不仅限于n=1情形；结果独立于β_m和n参数。

Conclusion: 现有暗物质直接探测实验（如XENONnT）可在无额外成本的情况下，对屏蔽暗能量模型中的变色龙粒子提供强约束，为天体物理和第五力搜索之外提供了互补的检验手段；未来多靶标和低阈值实验有助于区分变色龙粒子与其他轻标量粒子。

Abstract: We reassess prospects for direct detection of solar chameleons, in light of
recent progress in modeling their production, and the availability of new
XENONnT data. We show that the contribution from Primakoff production in the
electric fields of electrons and ions dominates the electron recoil event rate,
which is enhanced compared to earlier estimates based on magnetic conversion in
the tachocline alone. We argue that the signal is governed by the effective
coupling $\beta_{\text{eff}} \equiv \beta_{\gamma}M_e^{-4}$, which encodes the
combined effects of production and detection, where $\beta_{\gamma}$ and $M_e$
are the chameleon-photon (conformal) coupling and chameleon-electron disformal
coupling scale, respectively. Setting the height of the chameleon potential to
the dark energy (DE) scale $\Lambda \simeq 2.4\,{\text{meV}}$, we show that
XENONnT electron recoil data set the upper limit
$\log_{10}\beta_{\text{eff}}<-6.9$. This limit is independent of the conformal
matter coupling $\beta_m$ and index $n$, and applies to the whole class of
inverse power-law chameleons, well beyond the $n=1$ case usually studied. We
comment on how future multi-target experiments and lower-threshold analyses
could distinguish solar chameleons from other light (pseudo)scalar particles
such as axions. Our work demonstrates that existing dark matter direct
detection experiments can probe regions of parameter space relevant to screened
DE models, providing complementary tests to astrophysical and fifth-force
searches at no additional experimental cost.

</details>


### [80] [Light Scalars in Light of UV/IR Mixing: Classicalization via Synergy between Vainshtein & Chameleon Screenings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01739)
*Florian Nortier*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了通过经典化实现自洽紫外完成的标量场有效理论，强调了Vainshtein屏蔽和UV/IR混合对等级问题的影响，并指出需结合变色龙机制以保持经典子解的完整性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决无对称性情况下轻标量场理论中的等级问题，探索非威尔逊式的紫外完成机制。

Method: 回顾经典化的基础原理，使用简单的k-essence模型，分析标量势和费米子耦合对Vainshtein屏蔽的影响。

Result: 发现需要在标量质量与新共振态尺度之间保持小等级差异；变色龙屏蔽机制必须与Vainshtein屏蔽共存以维持经典子解的稳定。

Conclusion: 经典化提供了一种独特的UV/IR混合机制，有助于理解标量场理论中的层级问题和强耦合行为，且多种屏蔽机制可能共同作用于实际物理系统。

Abstract: Effective field theories featuring light scalar fields play a pivotal role in
addressing fundamental questions in (astro)particle physics and cosmology.
However, such theories often confront hierarchy problems in the absence of a
symmetry. Self-completion via classicalization offers a non-Wilsonian approach
to ultraviolet (UV) completion, wherein new scalar self-interactions involving
derivatives give rise to Vainshtein-like screening around energy-momentum
sources. Rather than introducing new UV degrees of freedom to restore unitarity
at high energies, these theories reshuffle their infrared (IR) degrees of
freedom by generating extended semi-classical objects -- referred to as
classicalons -- which decay into a multitude of soft particles. This mechanism
incorporates non-localizable fields, thereby realizing a form of UV/IR mixing
that is analogous to the dynamics of black holes in gravitational theories. In
this article, having reviewed the fundamental principles of classicalization
with a simple k-essence model, we then argue the necessity of maintaining a
little hierarchy between the scalar mass and the scale of the first new
resonances, thereby illustrating the impact of UV/IR mixing on hierarchy
problems. Additionally, we investigate the effects of a scalar potential and
couplings to fermions on the Vainshtein screening mechanism. We discuss that a
chameleon-like screening mechanism must accompany the Vainshtein screening to
preserve the integrity of classicalon solutions.

</details>


### [81] [Form of axion in DFSZ models with $U(1)_{PQ}$ symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01781)

of the mass mixing matrix of $CP$-odd sector. After applying $PQ$ mechanism to

and reasonable physical state of axion. The constraint of $PQ$ charge in $DFSZ
- I$ model is also pointed out. Then, anomalous couplings of
axion-photon-photon is re-examined. Triple-couplings of axion with two fermions
are studied. The decay of and axion into a pair of photon is also considered
via re-normalizable interactions arising from kinetic terms of scalar fields.

### [82] [The double copy effective action: a quantum (chromodynamics) approach to space-time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01799)
*John Joseph M. Carrasco,Suna Zekioglu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的量子场论作用量构造框架，将规范不变的散射振幅作为基本数据，通过将色-动量对偶从振幅推广到算符层面，系统地构建双复制相容的作用量，并揭示了引力相互作用如何从规范理论结构中衍生出来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统拉格朗日形式强调离壳对称性和紧致性，往往掩盖了物理可观测量的在壳结构。作者旨在建立一个以物理振幅为核心、直接关联规范理论与引力的构造性框架。

Method: 将双复制理论中的色共轭振幅分子提升为量子算符，利用因子化的规范理论分量系统识别新型局域算符内容，并构造与双复制兼容的作用量。

Result: 成功展示了如何从规范理论组分系统构造爱因斯坦引力作用量√(-g)R的算符展开，并实现了从树图级振幅到作用量和渐近量子态层次的双复制实现，同时生成了受Z理论和开超弦启发的高阶导数算符。

Conclusion: 该方法为振幅与有效作用量之间建立了具体桥梁，提供了一种基于物理观测的EFT构建新范式，揭示了规范理论与引力在算符层次上的深层结构联系。

Abstract: Conventional Lagrangian formulations of gauge and gravity theories emphasize
compactness and off-shell symmetry. This often obscures the structure of
on-shell physical observables. In this work, we present a constructive
framework that elevates gauge-invariant scattering amplitudes to the defining
data for quantum field theory actions, including effective field theories.
Focusing on double-copy theories, we promote color-dual amplitude numerators to
quantum operators. This enables the systematic identification of novel local
operator content at each multiplicity and the construction of
double-copy-compatible actions. By applying this framework to the
well-established double-copy relationship between Einstein gravity and
Yang-Mills theory, which holds for all-multiplicity tree-level amplitudes, we
demonstrate a systematic path to constructing the operator expansion of
$\sqrt{-g}R$ from factorized gauge-theory components. This clarifies how
gravitational interactions can be understood as emerging from simpler
gauge-theoretic structures at the action level. This formalism extends
color-kinematics duality from amplitude data to operator constructions,
naturally realizing the double copy at the level of actions and asymptotic
quantum states. We illustrate the method with Yang-Mills theory, Einstein
gravity, and its application to generating higher-derivative operators inspired
by Z-theory and open superstring amplitudes. This work provides a concrete
bridge between structured amplitudes and effective actions, offering a
physically grounded alternative to traditional EFT basis-building. It reveals
at the operator level deep structural connections between gauge theory and
gravity (connections long recognized in scattering amplitudes) from fundamental
interactions to their quantum state descriptions and higher-derivative
extensions.

### [83] [Axionlike particle searches in short-baseline liquid scintillator neutrino detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01812)
*D. Aristizabal Sierra,L. Duque,O. Miranda,H. Nunokawa*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了使用短基线反应堆中微子实验（如JUNO-TAO或CLOUD）探测类轴子粒子（ALPs）的可能性，利用反β衰变以外的信号通道，通过分辨ALP相互作用产生的快慢光子信号实现对放射性本底的有效抑制，并有望完全探索MeV质量范围和10^{-8}量级电子耦合强度的参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找尚未被探索的类轴子粒子（ALPs）参数空间区域，特别是在MeV质量和极弱耦合下的物理信号，并利用现有大型液态闪烁体探测器的高灵敏度开展多物理目标研究。

Method: 基于JUNO-TAO或CLOUD类型的实验参数，分析ALP通过Primakoff-like或Compton-like过程产生，并通过axio-electric吸收和ALP衰变为光子/电子对进行探测；利用散射过程中约5 ns延迟的双信号结构以及与闪烁光和俄歇电子的符合事件来实现背景 discrimination。

Result: 发现ALP散射会产生一个即时光子信号和约5 ns后的延迟光子信号，衰变与吸收过程可形成可分辨的符合事件，从而有效区分放射性本底；模拟结果显示该技术可完全覆盖宇宙学三角区，并探测到MeV质量范围、ALP-电子耦合达10^{-8}的区域。

Conclusion: 短基线反应堆中微子实验凭借其高精度和强本底抑制能力，在搜索类轴子粒子方面具有独特优势，能够拓展当前未被探测的参数空间，是未来轻弱相互作用粒子搜索的重要平台。

Abstract: Short-baseline reactor neutrino experiments using large organic liquid
scintillator detectors provide an experimentally rich environment for precise
neutrino physics. Neutrino detection is done through inverse beta decay and
relies on prompt and delayed signals, which enable powerful background
discrimination. In addition to their neutrino program, they offer an ideal
experimental environment for other physics searches. Here we discuss the case
of axionlike particles (ALPs) produced by either Primakoff-like or Compton-like
processes. Their detection relies on the corresponding inverse processes,
axio-electric absorption and ALP decays to photon or electron pairs. Assuming
experimental parameter values broadly representative of JUNO-TAO or CLOUD we
show that scattering ALP processes involve a prompt photon signal component
followed by a delayed photon signal about 5 ns after. We point out that if
these signals can be resolved, this might allow for efficient ALP signal
discrimination against radioactive background. Likewise, coincident events from
ALP decays and scintillation light followed by Auger electrons from
axio-electric absorption might as well allow for background discrimination. We
determine sensitivities in both the nuclear and electron channels using as a
benchmark case an experimental setup resembling that of the CLOUD or JUNO-TAO
detectors. Our findings demonstrate that with efficient background
discrimination these type of technology has the capability to test regions in
parameter space not yet explored. In particular, the cosmological triangle can
be fully tested and regions of MeV ALP masses with ALP-electron couplings of
the order of $10^{-8}$ can be entirely explored.

TL;DR: 本文讨论了中子-反中子转换实验的两种方法，并指出传统方法在介质抑制效应上的假设可能带来巨大偏差，强调需要更广泛的唯象研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

beams and intranuclear transformation leading to matter instability in
large-mass detectors. Plans for next-generation searches make it timely to
highlight the complementarity, necessity, and limitations of each method.
Converting the bound neutron limit into one for free neutrons traditionally
utilizes nucleus-specific estimates of the in-medium suppression of $n
\rightarrow \bar n$, obtained within mean-field theory under a single-operator
assumption. This paper highlights how this suppression can be
scenario-dependent, which can lead to deviations from the standard approach
that can span several orders of magnitude. A further goal of the paper is to
point out the need for a broader phenomenology program for $n\rightarrow
\bar{n}$ that is akin to those developed for electric dipole moments and other
systems for which short-distance new physics must be studied in-medium.

### [85] [Constraining memory-burdened primordial black holes with graviton-photon conversion and binary mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01848)
*Po-Yan Tseng,Yu-Min Yeh*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了原始黑洞（PBHs）在记忆负担效应下的稳定蒸发，并提出两种探测早期半经典阶段PBHs的方案，通过引力子-光子转换和当前PBH合并过程限制其丰度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于记忆负担效应抑制了蒸发通量，传统观测难以探测轻质量PBH暗物质，因此需要新方法探测仍处于半经典蒸发阶段的PBHs。

Method: 提出了两个场景：一是利用再复合时期后引力子通过Gertsenshtein效应在宇宙丝状结构磁场中转化为光子；二是依赖当前PBH合并产生年轻半经典黑洞并释放未被抑制的辐射。计算了这两种场景下的星系外光子谱。

Abstract: The memory-burden effect stabilizes the evaporating Primordial Black Holes
(PBHs) before its complete decay. This also suppresses the evaporation flux via
the entropy factor to the $k$-th power and circumvents severely astrophysical
and cosmological constraints, such that it opens a new mass window for PBH Dark
Matter lighter than $10^{15}$ g which has entered the memory-burden phase in
the present epoch. In this study, we propose two scenarios to probe PBHs in the
earlier semiclassical phase that evaporate at unsuppressed rates. The first
scenario considers gravitons, emitted semiclassically from PBHs, propagating
across the recombination epoch, then the magnetic field in the cosmological
filaments converts them into photons via the Gertsenshtein effect. The second
scenario relies on the PBHs mergers today, reproducing young semiclassical
black holes with unsuppressed evaporation. We perform computations of the
extragalactic photon spectrum from PBHs emission according to these scenarios.
The upper limits on the fractional abundance of PBH are obtained by comparing
with the sensitivities of gamma-ray observations. The graviton-photon
conversion scenario excludes the mass window $7.5\times 10^5\,{\rm g} \leq
M_{\rm PBH}\leq 4.4\times 10^7\,{\rm g}$ with $f_{\rm PBH}\geq 1$ and $k=1$.
Meanwhile, the merging scenario, which is insensitive on $k$, restricts PBH
Dark Matter lighter than $2.2\times 10^{11}$ g.

### [86] [A cosmographic analysis using DESI-DR2 and strong lensing: I. Time-Delay measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00788)
*Darshan Kumar,Deepak Jain,Shobhit Mahajan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文结合最新的Ia型超新星、重子声波振荡和强引力透镜时间延迟数据，利用距离和规则进行宇宙学分析，结果显示对开放宇宙有一定偏好，但空间平坦宇宙仍在95%置信水平内兼容；引入DESI-DR2数据后约束 tighter 并略倾向闭合宇宙，而q₀和j₀与ΛCDM模型预期一致。

  <summary>Details</summary>

geometry and expansion of the universe without relying on a fiducial
cosmological model. In this work, we perform a cosmographic analysis by
combining the latest Type Ia supernova datasets (PantheonPlus, DESY5, and
Union3), baryon acoustic oscillation data from DESI-DR2, and updated time-delay
distances from strong lensing systems. The analyses using SGL with individual
SNIa datasets (SGL+PantheonPlus, SGL+DESY5, and SGL+Union3) indicate a
preference for an open universe, though they remain consistent with spatially
flat universe at the $95%$ confidence level. When DESI-DR2 data is included in
each combination, the constraints tighten and shift slightly toward a closed
universe, while flatness remains supported at the $68%$ confidence level. The
best-fit values of $q_0$ and $j_0$ agree with $\Lambda$CDM expectations within
$95%$ or $99%$ confidence depending on the dataset, whereas $s_0$ remains
weakly constrained in all cases. This work is the first in a series of two
companion papers on cosmography with DESI-DR2 and strong lensing.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The distance ratio derived from strong gravitational lensing systems,

baryon acoustic oscillation measurements from DESI-DR2, and updated strong
lensing distance ratios. The cosmographic series is expanded to fourth order in
the variable $y = z/(1+z)$ to constrain the deceleration, jerk, and snap
parameters $(q_0,~j_0,~s_0)$. The analysis utilizes the distance sum rule (DSR)
to provide an independent assessment of the spatial curvature parameter,
$\Omega_{k0}$, without assuming a specific dynamical model. Our results based
on SGL distance ratio measurements combined with individual supernova datasets
suggest a mild preference for an open universe, though a flat universe is
supported at the 95% confidence level. Further, the inclusion of DESI-DR2 data
in each combination provides tighter constraints on the parameters and confirms

results for $q_0$ and $j_0$ are consistent with $\Lambda$CDM predictions across
datasets, while the constraint on $s_0$ remains limited but improves with the
inclusion of DESI-DR2. This is the second and final paper in a two-part series.

halos to radio galaxy population, to create an accurate sky simulation in order
to examine the feasibility of multi-tracer techniques. We present an analysis

### [89] [Limits of self-interacting neutrinos from the BAO and CMB phase shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00800)
*Abbé M. Whitford,Cullan Howlett,Tamara M. Davis,David Camarena,Francis-Yan Cyr-Racine*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型中的中微子在早期宇宙中自由传播，会在BAO中留下独特的相位偏移；然而，新物理可能改变这一特征的形状，因此需要探究其对中微子自相互作用的约束能力。

Method: 构建了具有普遍自相互作用的简单模型，分析相位偏移的变化，并评估BAO和CMB数据对自相互作用强度的限制能力。

Result: 单独使用BAO数据难以精确约束中微子自相互作用，但结合CMB和BAO的相位偏移信号有望检测到新相互作用的影响。

Conclusion: 结合CMB和BAO数据中的相位偏移特征可为中微子自相互作用提供更可靠的限制，尤其是解决当前$G_{\mathrm{eff}}$宇宙学约束中的双峰问题，且该方法可推广至非普遍相互作用模型。

Abstract: Neutrinos with Standard Model interactions free-stream in the early Universe,
leaving a distinct phase shift in the pattern of baryon acoustic oscillations
(BAO). When isolated, this phase shift allows one to robustly infer the
presence of the cosmic neutrino background in BAO and cosmic microwave
background (CMB) data independently of other cosmological parameters. While in
the context of the Standard Model, this phase shift follows a known
scale-dependent relation, new physics in the cosmic neutrino background could
alter the overall shape of this feature. In this paper, we discuss how changes
in the neutrino phase shift could be used to constrain self-interactions among
neutrinos. We produce simple models for this phase-shift assuming universal
self-interactions, and use these in order to understand what constraining power
is available for the strength of such interactions in BAO and CMB data. We find
that, although challenging, it may be possible to use a detection of the phase
to put a more robust limit on the strength of the self-interaction,
$G_{\mathrm{eff}}$, which at present suffers from bimodality in cosmological
constraints. Our forecast analysis reveals that BAO data alone will not provide
the precision needed to tightly constrain self-interactions; however, the
combined analysis of the phase shift signature in both CMB and BAO can
potentially provide a way to detect the impact of new neutrino interactions.
Our results could be extended upon for models with non-universal interactions.

### [90] [The CatWISE2020 Quasar dipole: A Reassessment of the Cosmic Dipole Anomaly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00822)
*Masroor Bashir,Pravabati Chingangbam,Stephen Appleby*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文重新评估了基于CatWISE2020类星体目录的宇宙微波背景温度偶极矩与射电源计数偶极矩之间的异常差异，使用包含大尺度结构、巡天覆盖和选择函数等效应的模拟框架，发现尽管考虑多种系统误差后显著性从4.9σ降至约3.3σ，但该异常仍存在，无法完全由聚类偶极或遮罩模式耦合解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验宇宙学原理中的运动学解释是否成立，特别是通过Ellis-Baldwin测试验证CMB温度偶极与射电源计数偶极的一致性，并探讨近期观测到的高显著性异常是否真实存在。

Method: 利用FLASK模拟框架生成包含大尺度结构对数正态实数、类星体成团偏置、径向选择函数和实际天空覆盖的仿真数据，分析运动学偶极与内在聚类偶极、散粒噪声及巡天几何效应共同作用下的统计显著性。

Result: 在忽略聚类偶极时，运动学偶极超出的显著性为3.63σ；当考虑随机方向聚类偶极时为3.44σ；若聚类偶极与运动学方向一致，则降至3.27σ。表明异常虽减弱但仍显著，且不能仅由聚类或遮罩效应解释。

Conclusion: CatWISE2020中观测到的偶极异常即使在全面考虑系统误差后依然存在，提示可能需要进一步审视宇宙学原理的基本假设或存在未被完全理解的系统误差源。

Abstract: The cosmological principle, which asserts a statistically homogeneous and
isotropic universe on large scales, is a foundational assumption of the
standard cosmological model. A critical test of this principle involves the
kinematic interpretation of the Cosmic Microwave Background temperature dipole,
conventionally attributed to our peculiar motion relative to the cosmic rest
frame. The Ellis-Baldwin test provides a probe of this kinematic interpretation
by searching for a matching Doppler-driven dipole in the number counts of
extragalactic radio sources. Recent measurements from the CatWISE2020 quasar
catalog have reported a dipole amplitude significantly exceeding the kinematic
expectation, with a claimed significance of $4.9\sigma$. We present a
comprehensive reassessment of this test using the same dataset, incorporating
major sources of uncertainty in the statistical inference. We use a simulation
framework based on the FLASK package, incorporating lognormal realizations of
the large-scale structure, the quasar clustering bias, the survey's radial
selection function, and its exact sky coverage. Our simulations account for the
kinematic dipole, the intrinsic clustering dipole, shot noise, and survey
geometry effects. The analysis yields a revised significance of the kinematic
dipole excess of $3.63\sigma$ in the absence of a clustering dipole, and
$3.44\sigma$ in the presence of a randomly oriented clustering dipole. When the
clustering dipole is aligned with the kinematic dipole direction, the
significance decreases further to $3.27\sigma$. Our analysis demonstrates that
although the anomaly is reduced in significance, it cannot be explained solely
as a result of the clustering dipole or mode coupling arising from the survey
mask.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Precise estimation of cosmological parameters from the cosmic microwave
background (CMB) remains a central goal of modern cosmology and a key test of
inflationary physics. However, this task is fundamentally limited by strong

faint CMB B-mode polarization signal. In this Letter, we introduce a fast,
simulation-based, end to end pipeline that integrates a robust component
separation technique with machine-learning, leading to cosmological parameter
estimation. Our approach combines the Analytical Blind Separation (ABS) method
for foreground removal with a neural network (NN) framework optimized to
extract cosmological parameters directly from full-sky simulations. We assess

satellite missions, designed to detect CMB B modes with unprecedented
sensitivity. Applying the pipeline to realistic sky simulations, we obtain 1

and 0.005 (LiteBIRD) and 0.0014 (PICO) for the tensor-to-scalar ratio, r. In
all cases, the recovered parameters are consistent with input values within 1
sigma across most of the parameter space. Results for LiteBIRD are in excellent
agreement with the latest forecasts from the collaboration. Our findings
establish this combined ABS-NN pipeline as a competitive, accurate, and
computationally efficient alternative for cosmological parameter inference,
offering a powerful framework for forthcoming CMB experiments.

### [93] [Galaxy assembly bias in cosmological hydrodynamical simulations: a comparison between SIMBA and IllustrisTNG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01441)
*Hong-Gang Yang,Marcos Pellejero,John Peacock,Romeel Davé*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了两种最先进的宇宙学流体动力学模拟（SIMBA和IllustrisTNG）中重子物理对星系组装偏差（GAB）强度及其红移演化的影响，发现GAB在z=5到z=2期间从约0%增加到5%，之后趋势分化：TNG中GAB持续增加至z=0时的10%，而SIMBA中则下降至接近0；进一步分析表明，GAB主要由大尺度密度环境（δ₅）驱动，潮汐各向异性贡献可忽略，并提出了一种基于晕占据分布（HOD）的密度依赖性GAB参数化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解星系组装偏差（GAB）的起源及其受重子物理影响的程度，对于精确建模大尺度结构和星系形成至关重要。现有模拟中GAB的演化存在差异，需探究其背后机制。

Method: 利用SIMBA和IllustrisTNG最大规模的宇宙学流体动力学模拟，通过按恒星质量选择星系并与同类质量暗晕中随机重分配的样本进行 clustering 对比来量化GAB；进一步在固定晕质量和大尺度环境（δ₅和α₅）内打乱星系以分离环境效应，并结合晕占据分布（HOD）模型分析中心星系与卫星星系对GAB的贡献。

Result: GAB在z=5时接近零，上升至z=2时约5%；此后TNG中继续增至z=0时10%，而SIMBA中回落至近零；GAB主要源于大尺度物质过密度（δ₅），潮汐各向异性（α₅）贡献可忽略；HOD分析显示中心星系和卫星星系数量仅在其对应的开启质量附近随过密度变化，高质晕内星系含量几乎不受环境影响。

Conclusion: 重子物理显著影响GAB的红移演化趋势，不同模拟中表现出的不同行为反映了其对反馈模型的敏感性；GAB主要由大尺度密度环境驱动，且集中在特定质量范围的星系；提出的HOD参数化方案可有效纳入密度依赖的GAB效应，提升星系-晕关联模型的准确性。

Abstract: Modelling of large-scale structure is increasingly concerned with galaxy
assembly bias (GAB), the dependence of galaxy clustering on quantities other
than halo mass. We investigate how baryonic physics affects the strength and
redshift evolution of GAB using the largest runs of two state-of-the-art
cosmological hydrodynamical simulations: SIMBA and IllustrisTNG. We quantify
GAB by comparing the clustering of stellar-mass-selected galaxies to that of
shuffled samples, where galaxies are randomly reassigned to haloes of similar
mass. We find that GAB in both simulations increases from approximately zero at
$z=5$ to a $\sim\,5\%$ change in clustering amplitude at $z=2$. After this
epoch, the trends diverge: GAB in TNG continues to increase, reaching
$\sim\,10\%$ at $z=0$, while in SIMBA it decreases to nearly zero. By further
shuffling galaxies within bins of halo mass and cosmic environment --
characterised by smoothed matter overdensity ($\delta_5$) and tidal anisotropy
($\alpha_5$) -- we show that most of the GAB in both simulations can be
attributed to the overdensity, while tidal anisotropy contributes negligibly in
both simulations. Exploring this effect from the point of view of the halo
occupation distribution (HOD), we find that numbers of central and satellite
galaxies vary with overdensity -- but only near the respective turn-on masses
for these two constituents: the galaxy contents of high-mass haloes are very
nearly independent of environment. We present a simple parameterisation that
allows the HOD modelling to be modified to reflect this form of
density-dependent GAB.

### [94] [Is $Λ$CDM on the run? Reconciling the CMB with the Lyman-$α$ Forest](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01612)
*Malcolm Fairbairn,Lucien Heurtier,María Olalla Olea-Romacho*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现>2σ的非零α_s和/或β_s迹象，表明原初功率谱具有显著的尺度依赖性；包含局部凹陷、凸起或振荡的暴涨势能模型更符合观测数据。

Abstract: We present new constraints on the scale dependence of the primordial power

data, extending sensitivity to smaller comoving scales. While ACT results
previously indicated a mild preference for positive running of the spectral
index, our joint analysis constrains both the running $\alpha_s$ and its
running $\beta_s$. Including eBOSS markedly tightens these constraints,
yielding a $>2\sigma$ indication of nonzero $\alpha_s$ and/or $\beta_s$,

### [95] [Dynamical Dark Energy from a Massive Vector Field in Generalized Proca Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01700)
*Abhi Savaliya*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一个包含大质量宇宙矢量场的理论框架，通过非最小耦合背景曲率来解释DESI DR2数据中观测到的偏离ΛCDM模型的现象，该模型在当前宇宙加速膨胀中表现出与观测一致的动力学暗能量行为，并在未来晚期趋近于ΛCDM行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受DESI DR2观测数据显示可能偏离标准ΛCDM宇宙学的启发，试图构建一个能解释这一现象的理论模型。

Method: 构建一个大质量宇宙矢量场Bμ非最小耦合背景曲率的理论框架，并分析其有效状态方程参数w(\tilde H)，寻找与当前宇宙学观测一致的参数空间区域。

Result: 发现参数空间中的狭窄区域与DESI等观测数据一致，得到耦合常数λ<2.98×10^-11、质量范围3.1356×10^-66 g ≤ m ≤ 3.3627×10^-66 g，以及log₁₀\tildeγ在-0.405到-0.38之间，对应的当前状态方程偏差δ在0.107至0.217范围内。

Conclusion: 所提出的矢量场框架能够合理解释DESI揭示的ΛCDM偏离现象，并建立了模型参数与观测暗能量动力学之间的直接联系，且在晚期宇宙中趋于ΛCDM行为。

Abstract: In this paper, we emphasise the recent observational findings from the Dark
Energy Spectroscopic Instrument Data Release 2 (DESI DR2), which provide
compelling evidence for a possible deviation from the standard $\Lambda$CDM
(Cold Dark Matter) cosmology, suggesting the presence of a dynamically evolving
effective dark energy component. Motivated by this, we construct a theoretical
framework in which a massive cosmological vector field, $B^{\mu}$, couples
non-minimally to the background curvature through marginal interactions,
offering a controlled mechanism to realise the deviation from the $\Lambda$CDM
model. A detailed analysis of the effective Equation of State (EoS) parameter
$w(\tilde H)$ reveals a narrow region of parameter space consistent with
current cosmological observations presented by DESI. The analysis yields a
stringent upper bound for the coupling constant $\lambda$ to be
$\lambda<2.98\times10^{-11}$, a very strong bound on mass
$3.1356\times10^{-66}~\text{g} \leq m \leq 3.3627\times10^{-66}~\text{g},$ and
the admissible range $-0.405 \leq \log_{10}\tilde\gamma \leq -0.38$ for which
present-day value $w_0 = w(\tilde H = 1)$ corresponding to a deviation $\delta
= w_0 + 1$ that lies within the region $0.107 \leq \delta \leq 0.217$. This
interval reproduces the deviation inferred from the combined DESI, Cosmic
Microwave Background (CMB), and Pantheon+ data, reflecting a controlled
departure from the $\Lambda$CDM behaviour. In summary, the results suggest that
the proposed framework of a massive vector field can account for the departure
from $\Lambda$CDM behaviour highlighted by DESI in the current cosmic
acceleration. Furthermore, the framework approaches the $\Lambda$CDM behaviour
in late-time $t\gtrsim28$ Gyr, establishing a direct phenomenological link
between the underlying parameters and the observed dynamical nature of dark
energy.

</details>


### [96] [Gravitational Wave Spectral Shapes as a probe of Long Lived Right-handed Neutrinos, Leptogenesis and Dark Matter: Gobal versus Local B-L Cosmic Strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01779)
*Satyabrata Datta,Anish Ghoshal,Angus Spalding,Graham White*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了在U(1)_{B-L}对称性框架下，Type-I、II、III型跷跷板机制中右手中微子（RHN）导致的早期物质主导时期及其对引力波谱的影响，发现仅在Type-I模型中，长寿命RHN可引发早期物质主导，产生可观测的引力波特征（如拐点和断点），这些特征可用于直接确定RHN质量M和有效中微子质量\tilde m，并探讨了其对暗物质生成和轻子生成的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释跷跷板机制尺度远高于电弱尺度的自然性问题，并探索U(1)_{B-L}对称性破缺后产生的宇宙弦及引力波信号，尤其是早期非辐射主导时期可能带来的独特引力波谱特征。

Method: 在Type-I、II、III跷跷板模型中分析RHN的动力学行为，结合宇宙学演化模拟，研究热产生RHN是否能导致早期物质主导，并计算其对引力波谱的影响，同时推导引力波频率与中微子参数及暗物质、重子丰度之间的解析与半解析关系。

Result: 仅在Type-I模型中，长寿命RHN可在部分参数空间引发早期物质主导，导致引力波谱出现明显拐点和断点；LISA和ET等探测器可探测到M∈[0.1,10^9] GeV和\tilde m∈[10^{-10},10^{-8}] eV范围内的RHN信号；并确定了成功轻子生成和不对称暗物质生成的可行参数空间。

Conclusion: Type-I seesaw模型中的长寿命右手中微子可通过早期物质主导在引力波谱中留下可探测特征，为中微子质量、暗物质和重子不对称性提供统一解释，且未来引力波观测有望直接验证该机制。

Abstract: The scale of the seesaw mechanism is typically much larger than the
electroweak scale. This hierarchy can be naturally explained by $U(1)_{B-L}$
symmetry, which after spontaneous symmetry breaking, simultaneously generates
Majorana masses for neutrinos and produces a network of cosmic strings. Such
strings generate a gravitational wave (GW) spectrum which is expected to be
almost uniform in frequency unless there is a departure from the usual early
radiation domination. We explore this possibility in Type I, II and III seesaw
frameworks, finding that only for Type-I, long-lived right-handed neutrinos
(RHN) may provide a period of early matter domination for parts of the
parameter space, even if they are thermally produced. Such a period leaves
distinctive imprints in the GW spectrum in the form of characteristic breaks
and a knee feature, arising due to the end and start of the periods of RHN
domination. These features, if detected, directly determine the mass $M$, and
effective neutrino mass $\tilde m$ of the dominating RHN. We find that GW
detectors like LISA and ET could probe RHN masses in the range
$M\in[0.1,10^{9}]$ GeV and effective neutrino masses in the $\tilde
m\in[10^{-10},10^{-8}]$ eV range. We investigate the phenomenological
implications of long-lived right-handed neutrinos for both local and global
$U(1)_{B-L}$ strings, focusing on dark matter production and leptogenesis. We
map the viable and detectable parameter space for successful baryogenesis and
asymmetric dark matter production from right-handed neutrino decays. We derive
analytical and semi-analytical relations correlating the characteristic
gravitational-wave frequencies to the neutrino parameters $\tilde m$ and $M$,
as well as to the relic abundances of dark matter and baryons.

</details>

final cosmological theory and they are anxious to see it replaced by something
better! After reviewing some of the impactful events in cosmology since the
last \Le Workshop, I focus on the role that the recent evidence for evolving
dark energy may play in getting cosmology that better theory.

### [98] [Conserved Quantities in Expanding Gödel Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00238)
*Alexander Leithes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究了包含膨胀和旋转的Gödel背景时空的线性扰动，构造了规范不变量，并发现压力为零的尘埃在大尺度上存在守恒量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索扩展Gödel宇宙学中扰动的变换行为，并寻找守恒量。

Method: 通过扰动能量守恒方程分析扰动的规范变换性质，构建规范不变量。

Result: 发现了在压力为零的尘埃情况下，空间度规迹扰动ζSMTP在大尺度上是守恒的。

Conclusion: 在Expanding Gödel宇宙学中存在大尺度守恒量，未来计划将研究推广到完美流体情形。

Abstract: At linear order we study perturbations to a G\"odel background spacetime
which includes expansion in addition to rotation. We investigate the
transformation behaviour of these perturbations under gauge transformations and
construct gauge invariant quantities. Using the perturbed energy conservation
equation we find that there are conserved quantities in Expanding G\"odel (EG)
Cosmology, in particular a spatial metric trace perturbation, {\zeta} SMTP ,
which is conserved on large scales for pressureless dust. We intend to extend
our discussion to a perfect fluid matter content with a view to also obtaining
conserved quantities in this context.

### [99] [Spin-up and mass-gain in hyperbolic encounters of spinning black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00307)
*Healey Kogan,Frederick C. L. Pardoe,Helvi Witek*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究通过数值相对论模拟，探讨了等质量黑洞在不同初始自旋、动量和入射角下的散射过程中自旋增加和质量增益的现象，发现接近散射与合并阈值的系统通常具有最大的自旋和质量增长，且初始自旋为负时效应更显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解黑洞在引力波辐射中重新吸收角动量和能量导致的自旋和质量变化机制，特别是在散射过程中的动力学行为。

Method: 使用数值相对论方法，对初始自旋范围为[-0.7, 0.7]、不同动量和入射角的等质量黑洞系统进行了一系列模拟，识别散射与合并的临界角度，并分析自旋和质量的变化。

Result: 自旋增加和质量增益在接近临界入射角、高动量和反向初始自旋时最大；自旋增加随初始自旋线性减少；初始自旋为0.7时可能出现自旋下降现象；最大自旋增加达0.3，最大质量增加达15%。

Conclusion: 黑洞散射过程中的自旋和质量演化强烈依赖于初始配置，特别是入射角和初始自旋方向，揭示了非线性引力动力学中的复杂能量-角动量交换机制。

Abstract: Scattering black holes spin up and gain mass through the re-absorption of
orbital angular momentum and energy radiated in gravitational waves during
their encounter. In this work, we perform a series of numerical relativity
simulations to investigate the spin-up and mass-gain for equal-mass black holes
with a wide range of equal initial spins, $\chi_{\rm i}\in[-0.7,0.7]$, aligned
(or anti-aligned) to the orbital angular momentum. We also consider a variety
of initial momenta. Furthermore, we explore a range of incident angles and
identify the threshold between scattering and merging configurations. The
spin-up and mass-gain are typically largest in systems with incident angles
close to the threshold value, large momenta, and negative (i.e. anti-aligned)
initial spins. When evaluated at the threshold angle, we find that the spin-up
decreases linearly with initial spin. Intriguingly, systems with initial spin
$\chi_{\rm i}=0.7$ sometimes experience a spin-down, in spite of an increase in
the black-hole angular momentum, due to a corresponding gain in the black-hole
mass. Across the simulation suite, we find a maximum spin-up of $0.3$ and a
maximum increase in the black-hole mass of $15\%$.

</details>

Abstract: A new thermal view of scalar-tensor gravity, in which general relativity is

formalism, results on the convergence to Einstein cosmology (or lack thereof)
are first obtained for general $f(R)$ theories, and then illustrated with

### [101] [Effective spacetime description of light propagation in linear magnetoelectric media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00353)
*Lucas T. de Paula,Caio C. Holanda Ribeiro,Vitorio A. De Lorenci*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过将麦克斯韦方程组协变形式应用于线性磁电介质，构建了光传播的有效时空模型，并揭示了其与引力现象的类比，特别是在几何光学极限下可形成类似事件视界的单向传播区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索引力与光学现象之间的形式类比已有百年历史，本文旨在利用这一类比，从有效时空的角度研究线性磁电介质中的光传播特性。

Method: 从协变形式的麦克斯韦方程出发，推导出适用于线性、非色散磁电材料的有效度规，并在几何光学极限下构建类比模型。

Result: 证明了在线性非色散磁电材料中总能定义一个有效度规，并发现当磁电响应达到合理强度时，可形成类似事件视界的单向传播区域。

Conclusion: 该研究深化了对广义相对论运动学特性的理解，并为模拟黑洞等引力现象提供了新的光学平台。

Abstract: Formal analogies between gravitational and optical phenomena have been
explored for over a century, providing valuable insights into kinematic aspects
of general relativity. Here, this analogy is employed to study light
propagation in linear magnetoelectric media from an effective spacetime
perspective. Starting from Maxwell's equations in covariant form, it is shown
that an effective metric can always be identified for linear, non-dispersive
magnetoelectric materials. The effective metric is then used to construct
analog models in the limit of geometric optics. Among the optical effects
analyzed, it is shown that under reasonable assumptions on the magnitude of the
magnetoelectric response, a one-way propagation region can be established,
which behaves analogously to an event horizon.

### [102] [Structural Properties of Magnetized Neutron Stars under f (R, T ) Gravity Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00425)
*Charul Rathod,M. Mishra,Prasanta Kumar Das*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在f(R,T)修正引力框架下强磁场对中子星结构特性的影响，通过求解修正的TOV方程并使用APR、FPS和SLy状态方程，发现更负的修正引力参数会增加中子星的最大引力质量，而强中心磁场仅轻微降低最大质量且不破坏球对称性，结果与GW170817、PSR和NICER观测数据一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在高密度物质条件下修正引力理论对中子星结构性质的影响，特别是在存在强磁场的情况下，检验f(R,T)引力模型相对于广义相对论的偏离及其对天体物理观测的解释能力。

Method: 采用各向同性状态方程（APR、FPS、SLy），数值求解f(R,T)引力框架下的修正Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff方程，计算不同修正引力参数和中心磁场强度下的质量-半径关系及质量和压力分布。

Result: 更负的修正引力参数导致更高的最大引力质量；高达10^18高斯的强中心磁场仅引起最大质量轻微下降，且未破坏球对称性；所得结果与GW170817、PSR和NICER的观测数据相符。

Conclusion: 在f(R,T)修正引力框架下，强磁场对中子星结构影响较小，而修正引力参数显著影响其最大质量，表明该理论模型能较好地解释当前中子星观测数据。

Abstract: The current work investigates the structural properties of neutron stars in
the presence of a strong magnetic field within the framework of f(R,T) modified
gravity, where the matter-geometry coupling leads to deviations from general
relativity at high matter densities. We present here the mass-radius sequences,
as well as the mass and pressure distributions for various values of the
modified gravity parameter and the central magnetic field. The modified
Tolman-Oppenheimer- Volkoff equations are numerically solved using isotropic
equations of state, specifically the APR, FPS, and SLy models. Comparing the
corresponding results in the context of general relativity suggests that more
negative values of the modified gravity parameter result in higher maximum
gravitational masses. In contrast, strong central magnetic fields of up to 1018
Gauss cause only a slight decrease in maximum mass without disrupting spherical
symmetry. Our findings are in agreement with the observed data from GW170817,
PSR and NICER.

### [103] [Reconstructing $f(T)$ Gravity From Hubble Parameterization Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00464)
*Suraj Kumar Behera,Pratik P. Ray,B. Mishra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了基于挠率引力理论$f(T)$的宇宙学模型，用于描述宇宙晚期的加速膨胀。通过引入一个参数化的哈勃参数，并利用宇宙学数据约束自由参数，分析了减速度、jerk和snap等几何参数，并与观测值对比。研究还探讨了非线性$f(T)$形式下的动力学行为和能量条件，发现强能量条件被违反，表明宇宙具有晚期的phantom特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用一种具有良好物理动机的哈勃参数参数化方法，在$f(T)$引力理论下建立宇宙学模型，并利用观测数据（如SNIa、BAO等）对模型自由参数进行约束，进而分析相关几何和动力学参数。

Result: 成功构建了一个符合当前观测数据的$f(T)$宇宙学模型；得到的模型显示宇宙处于晚期加速膨胀阶段；计算出的减速度、jerk和snap参数与观测建议值一致；发现强能量条件被违反，支持phantom型演化行为。

Conclusion: 在$f(T)$引力理论中，所提出的模型能够有效描述宇宙晚期的加速膨胀，并呈现出phantom态的行为特征，为替代广义相对论中的暗能量提供了可能路径。

Abstract: In this paper, we have presented the cosmological model of the Universe that
represents late time cosmic acceleration in torsion based gravitational theory,
the $f(T)$ gravity. A well motivated parametrization for the Hubble parameter
has been introduced and the free parameters involved are constrained using the
cosmological datasets. With the constrained values of the free parameters,
other geometrical parameters such as deceleration parameter, jerk parameter,
and snap parameter are analyzed and confronted with the prescribed value of the
cosmological observations. In addition, the dynamical parameters are analyzed
in some non-linear form of $f(T)$ and the energy conditions are also studied
and confirmed with the violation of the strong energy condition. The obtained
cosmological model provides late time phantom behavior of the Universe.

</details>


### [104] [Testing general relativity with gravitational waves -- improving and extending Modified Dispersion Relation tests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00497)
*Tomasz Baka,Balázs Cirok,K. Haris,Johannes Noller,N. V. Krishnendu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文改进了对引力波色散关系的检验方法，包括群速度参数化、更好的采样方法以及扩展到负指数项，并利用GWTC-3数据重新分析，显著改善了单个事件的后验结果，联合约束也略有提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了更精确地检验广义相对论，特别是通过引力波数据探测可能存在的引力子质量或洛伦兹对称性破缺效应。

Method: 引入群速度参数化、优化采样方法，并将色散关系中的动量幂律项扩展至负指数α，应用于GWTC-3中的引力波事件进行重新分析。

Result: 相比GWTC-3的结果，单个事件的后验分布显著改善，整体后验宽度平均缩小19%；引力子质量的90%上限从2.42×10⁻¹¹ peV降至2.21×10⁻¹¹ peV；对于α为-1、-2、-3的情况未发现偏离广义相对论的证据。

Conclusion: 改进的方法提升了对修正色散关系的限制精度，当前数据仍支持广义相对论，未发现洛伦兹对称性破缺或非零引力子质量的证据。

Abstract: Searching for a modified dispersion relation is one of the general relativity
tests performed by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA collaboration with each new cumulative
Gravitational Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC). It considers classes of theories
that modify the dispersion of gravitational waves by introducing a massive
graviton or breaking Lorentz invariance. The symmetry breaking is parameterized
phenomenologically by a momentum power law term $p^\alpha$ added to the
dispersion relation, with the test placing constraints on the amplitude
$A_\alpha$ of the introduced deviation. In this work, we implement improvements
to the test, chief among them group velocity parametrization, a better sampling
procedure, and extension to negative exponents $\alpha$ of $p$. We then
reanalyze the events from the third catalog, GWTC-3, with our improved method.
Compared with GWTC-3 results, we find significant improvement, mostly from the
improved sampling method, in the posteriors obtained by analyzing individual
event and more modest improvements in the combined bounds on amplitude
parameters $A_\alpha$ -- on average, we observe 19% shrinking of posterior
width. The 90% upper bound on the graviton mass changes from $2.42 \times
10^{-11}$ peV to $2.21 \times 10^{-11}$ peV. For the extension of our test to
$\alpha \in \{-1, -2, -3\}$, we find no evidence in favor of general relativity
violation.

</details>


### [105] [Reflectionless and echo modes in asymmetric Damour-Solodukhin wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00565)
*Wei-Liang Qian,Qiyuan Pan,Ramin G. Daghigh,Bean Wang,Rui-Hong Yue*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了超紧凑物体中回声现象的两种模式——渐近高阶准正规模（回声模式）和无反射散射模式之间的相似性，通过解析方法证明它们在复频率平面上具有类似的渐近特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解回声波形的本质及其产生机制，澄清准正规模与无反射模式在描述回声现象中的角色争议。

Method: 扩展无反射模式的定义至完全无反射情况，并将对称Damour-Solodukhin虫洞推广到非对称情形，利用散射矩阵和格林函数两种方法进行分析。

Result: 发现回声模式与无反射模式在复频率平面上的渐近分布高度相似，实部在高频极限下重合，且模式间距一致；对称虫洞的无反射模式位于实轴上，偏离实轴的程度反映虫洞的不对称性。

Conclusion: 回声现象可用回声模式或无反射模式有效描述，二者在渐近极限下具有一致性，支持了不同视角下对回声机制的理解。

Abstract: It is understood that the echo waveforms in ultracompact objects can be
regarded as composed mainly of the asymptotic high-overtone quasinormal modes,
dubbed echo modes, which predominantly lie parallel to the real frequency axis.
Alternatively, Rosato {\it et al.} recently suggested that high-frequency
quasi-reflectionless scattering modes are primarily responsible for the echo
phenomenon. This identification relies on greybody factors as stable
observables, despite the apparent spectral instability of quasinormal modes. In
this work, by extending the definition of quasi-reflectionless modes to
reflectionless ones and generalizing symmetric Damour-Solodukhin wormholes to
asymmetric cases, we examine the underlying similarity between the
reflectionless and echo mode spectra in the complex frequency plane. Through a
primarily analytical treatment, we demonstrate that the asymptotic properties
of these two spectra exhibit a strong resemblance, featuring an approximately
uniform distribution parallel to the real frequency axis with the same spacing
between successive modes. Specifically, the real parts of echo modes coincide
with those of reflectionless modes at the limit $|\mathrm{Re}\omega| \gg
|\mathrm{Im}\omega|$. While echo modes typically possess non-vanishing
imaginary parts, the reflectionless modes of symmetric Damour-Solodukhin
wormholes lie precisely on the real frequency axis, with any deviation serving
as a measure of the degree of asymmetry of the wormhole. We support our
derivations by employing two complementary approaches, based on the scattering
matrix and the Green's function, and argue that both perspectives provide
effective tools for describing the echo phenomenon.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Weyl共形变换，在满足解析性的无限多共形框架下分析Bianchi IX时空，研究质量为零、非零及共形耦合粒子的测地线行为，验证时空的测地完备性。

Result: 证明在所选共形框架下，Bianchi IX时空的初态与末态奇点均无法在有限仿射参数或固有时内达到，实现了测地完备；同时共形重标度将Bianchi IX度规变为类FLRW形式，抑制了奇点附近的混沌振荡。

Abstract: We hereby address the cosmological singularity problem in a general

particular, we focus on the Bianchi IX spacetime and we show that both the
initial (big bang) and final (big crunch) singularities disappear in an
infinite class of conformal frames naturally selected according to analyticity.
It turns out that the past and future singularities are both unattainable
within a finite affine parameter (for massless particles) or within a finite
proper time (for massive and conformally coupled particles). In order to prove
such a statement, we show the geodesic completion of the spacetime when probed
by massless, massive, and conformally coupled particles. Finally, the chaotic
behavior of the spacetime near the singularity is tamed by a conformal
rescaling that turns the Bianchi IX metric into a quasi-FLRW spacetime.

magnitude, restoring the peak of quasi-normal mode(QNM) in the time-frequency

foundation for the following scientific work.

Abstract: We study the dynamics of a massive scalar field in the background of the
Hayward black hole, which can be interpreted both as a regular spacetime and as
an effective geometry arising from Asymptotically Safe gravity. The quasinormal
spectrum and grey-body factors are computed using the WKB method with Pad\'e
improvements and confirmed through time-domain integration followed by Prony
analysis. We find that the mass of the field significantly suppresses the

decaying ringdown is replaced by oscillatory tails with a power-law envelope.
The corresponding grey-body factors reveal a pronounced shift of the

precision as either the field mass increases or the multipole number decreases.

### [111] [Analytical sensitivity curves of the second-generation time-delay interferometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01330)
*Chunyu Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现第二代TDI组合与其第一代具有相同灵敏度；A、E、T通道的灵敏度与TDI代际无关；A和E通道性能相当，T通道在低频段较弱；多数组合的灵敏度曲线在特定频段呈平坦；ζ组合与T通道性能成比例。

Abstract: Forthcoming space-based gravitational-wave (GW) detectors will employ
second-generation time-delay interferometry (TDI) to suppress laser frequency
noise and achieve the sensitivity required for GW detection. We introduce an

same sensitivities as their first-generation counterparts; (ii) the $A, E, T$
sensitivities and the optimal sensitivity are independent of the TDI generation
and specific combination; (iii) the $A$ and $E$ channels have equal averaged
responses, noise PSDs, and sensitivities, while the $T$ channel has much weaker
response and sensitivity at low frequencies ($2\pi fL/c\lesssim3$); (iv) except
for the $(\alpha,\beta,\gamma)$ and $\zeta$ combinations and the $T$ channel,

proof-mass- and optical-path-dominated regimes, while the response-transition
frequency $\sim 1.5/(2\pi L/c)$ separates the response function's low- and

and data-analysis studies for future space-based GW detectors.

Method: 引入无量纲几何因子 $f(\theta, \phi)$ 描述辐射不透明度的角依赖性，结合爱因斯坦场方程分析坍缩动力学，推导方向相关的阈值条件。

Conclusion: 恒星坍缩的最终状态可通过几何因子和预计算的不透明度表进行系统分析，为理解强磁化致密天体的演化提供了新理论工具。

Abstract: The final fate of a collapsing star depends not only on how much matter it
contains but also on how that matter resists gravity in different directions.
In this work, we investigate the final fate of highly magnetized
radiation-dominated spherically symmetric dissipative stellar configurations.
We study the dynamics of collapse by introducing a dimensionless geometric
factor $f(\theta, \phi)$ defined by the angular dependence of the radiative
opacity. Using the field equations, we derive direction-sensitive threshold
conditions that determine whether collapse initiates, halts, or reverses. The
resulting inequalities unify black hole formation, bounce behavior, and delayed
trapping of geodesics into a single geometrically controlled framework. This
theoretical analysis would help analyze the collapse through pre-computed
opacity tables for different magnetic field, temperature, and density profiles,
along with other data available for such considered profiles.

</details>

Abstract: This paper develops a systematic approach to the geometrization of dynamics
