### [124] [Robustness of timelike circular orbit topology against particle spin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01447)
*Yong Song,Jiaqi Fu,Yiting Cen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon形式和Tulczyjew自旋补充条件，研究了静态球对称时空中自旋测试粒子的类时圆轨道（TCO）的拓扑性质。通过构造赤道面上的辅助势和向量场，计算了不同黑洞时空中外 horizon 间及外部区域的拓扑卷绕数W。结果表明，在相邻两个视界之间W=-1，存在至少一个不稳定的TCO；在渐近平坦和AdS黑洞最外视界之外W=0，意味着TCO必须成对出现（稳定-不稳定）或不存在。该结论与粒子自旋方向无关，并在Schwarzschild、Schwarzschild-AdS和Schwarzschild-dS时空中得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究自旋测试粒子在强引力场中运动时，时空结构本身对其轨道稳定性的影响，特别是引入自旋后是否改变轨道存在的拓扑规律。

Method: 采用Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon方程结合Tulczyjew条件，在静态球对称时空中构建赤道面上的辅助势和向量场，利用拓扑卷绕数W分析类时圆轨道的存在性和稳定性。

Result: 在任意两个相邻视界之间（包括dS情况下的宇宙学视界），拓扑数W=-1，表明至少存在一个不稳定的TCO；在渐近平坦和AdS黑洞最外视界之外，W=0，说明TCO只能以稳定-不稳定对的形式出现或完全不存在。这些结果在Schwarzschild、Schwarzschild-AdS和Schwarzschild-dS时空中被具体验证。

Conclusion: 自旋测试粒子的类时圆轨道的拓扑性质由时空几何结构本身决定，拓扑卷绕数W揭示了轨道存在的普适规律，且不受粒子自旋方向影响，凸显了广义相对论中时空拓扑对动力学行为的根本作用。

Abstract: Based on a detailed study of the motion of spinning test particles within the
Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon formalism under the Tulczyjew spin-supplementary
condition in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes, we investigate the
topological properties of timelike circular orbits (TCOs) for such particles.
By constructing an auxiliary potential and an associated vector field on the
equatorial plane, we compute the topological winding number W for regions
between horizons and outside the outermost horizon in asymptotically flat,
anti-de Sitter (AdS), and de Sitter (dS) black hole spacetimes. Our results
show that between two neighboring horizons (including the cosmological horizon
in the dS case), the topological number is W=-1, indicating the presence of at
least one unstable TCO. Outside the outermost horizon, we find W=0 for both
asymptotically flat and AdS black holes, implying that any TCOs must appear in
stable-unstable pairs or be absent. These conclusions are independent of the
spin orientation (co-rotating or counter-rotating) of the test particle. The
analysis is supported by explicit examples in Schwarzschild, Schwarzschild-AdS,
and Schwarzschild-dS spacetimes, confirming the general topological
predictions. While the effective potential for spinning particles has been
previously studied, the topological approach employed here reveals invariant
properties that remain robust even when spin is included, thereby highlighting
the fundamental influence of the spacetime structure itself.

</details>


### [125] [The images of Brans-Dicke-Kerr type naked singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01478)
*Fen Long,Weike Deng,Xin Qin,Songbai Chen,Jiliang Jing*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究了Brans-Dicke-Kerr时空的图像，发现当参数ω>-3/2时表现为具有不同结构的裸奇点，其阴影随ω减小而变得更扁更小，尤其在ω<1/2时呈现“水母”状和自相似分形结构；当a>M时，赤道观测者会看到两个独立区域组成的灰色区域，可据此区分Kerr和Kerr-de Sitter情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Brans-Dicke理论中轴对称旋转解的成像特性，以揭示Brans-Dicke-Kerr时空的内在结构，并为通过高精度观测检验Brans-Dicke理论提供依据。

Method: 分析Brans-Dicke-Kerr时空在不同参数下的图像特征，特别是阴影形状和结构随Brans-Dicke参数ω的变化。

Result: 发现ω>-3/2时为裸奇点；ω减小导致阴影更扁更小；ω<1/2时出现‘水母’状和分形结构；a>M时出现双斑块灰色区域。

Conclusion: Brans-Dicke-Kerr时空的图像特征显著区别于Kerr和Kerr-de Sitter情况，可通过未来高精度观测验证Brans-Dicke理论。

Abstract: We have studied the images of the Brans-Dicke-Kerr spacetime with a
dimensionless Brans-Dicke parameter $\omega$, which belongs to axisymmetric
rotating solutions in the Brans-Dicke theory. Our results show that the
Brans-Dicke-Kerr spacetime with the parameter $\omega>-3/2$ represents naked
singularities with distinct structures. For the case with $a \leq M$, the
shadow in the Brans-Dicke-Kerr spacetime persists, gradually becomes flatter
and smaller as $\omega$ decreases. Especially when $\omega<1/2$, the shadow in
the image exhibit a very special ``jellyfish" shape and possesses a
self-similar fractal structure. For the case with $a > M$, a distinct gray
region consisting of two separate patches appears in the image observed by
equatorial observers. This indicating that the Brans-Dicke-Kerr spacetime can
be distinguished from the Kerr and Kerr-de Sitter cases based on its image.
These effects of the Brans-Dicke parameter could help us to reveal the
intrinsic structure of the Brans-Dicke-Kerr spacetimes and provide a foundation
for testing Brans-Dicke theory through future high-precision observations.

</details>


### [126] [Shadow of Extreme Compact Charged Objects in Consistent 4-Dimensional Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01533)
*Sara Saghafi,Kourosh Nozari,Maryam Kaveh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在四维Einstein Gauss Bonnet引力框架下的极端致密带电天体（ECCO），通过对比事件视界望远镜（EHT）的观测数据，限制Gauss Bonnet耦合常数α。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在极小和宇宙学尺度上更好地描述引力现象，需推广广义相对论；EGB理论是其中一种引入曲率修正的扩展。

Method: 研究EGB引力中ECCO时空的测地结构及其光学特性（如阴影、光线偏折角等可观测量），并与EHT观测数据对比。

Result: 获得了与EHT观测一致的EGB模型下ECCO的光学特征，并据此对Gauss Bonnet耦合常数α给出了约束。

Conclusion: 通过结合理论预测与EHT观测，可有效限制四维EGB引力中的耦合常数α，为修正引力理论提供观测依据。

Abstract: In order to better describe gravitational phenomena on both very small and
cosmological scales, there have been constant attempts to generalize and expand
the theory of General Relativity (GR) since its inception. The Einstein Gauss
Bonnet (EGB) theory is one such extension that adds spacetime corrections
related to curvature. Since the standard Gauss Bonnet term is purely
topological, it does not contribute to the field equations in four dimensions.
To get around this restriction, however, an invariant four dimensional limit
has been developed. In this work, we study Extreme Compact Charged Objects
(ECCOs), which can resemble black holes, in a gravity framework that is
compatible with Einstein Gauss Bonnet in four dimensions. Our main goal is to
compare theoretical predictions with Event Horizon Telescope (EHT)
observational data in order to constrain the Gauss Bonnet coupling constant
{\alpha}. In order to achieve this, we investigate important optical
characteristics like the shadow, light bending angle, and other associated
observables, as well as the geodesic structure of ECCO spacetimes in EGB
gravity. Finally, we apply these findings to constrain the Gauss Bonnet
constant.

</details>


### [127] [A General Framework for the Spontaneous Scalarization of Regular Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01544)
*Ernesto Contreras,Mikaela Carrasco-Hidalgo,Pedro Bargueño,Arthur G. Suvorov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由非线性电动力学支持的正则黑洞的自发标量化，提出了一种基于P对偶形式的通用框架，并以Balart-Vagenas黑洞为例，展示了标量化解在熵上更优且与观测兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非线性电动力学背景下正则黑洞的自发标量化机制，扩展以往仅限于Reissner-Nordström类解的研究范围。

Method: 采用P对偶形式重构电磁部分，并非最小耦合实标量场，基于任意种子度规构建标量化模型。

Result: 在Balart-Vagenas黑洞中发现标量化与无标量分支共存，且标量化态熵更大；黑洞阴影和准正规模存在小于10%的可观测偏差。

Conclusion: 该框架为在非线性电动力学时空中研究标量化提供了普适途径，且此类解尚未被当前电磁和引力波观测排除。

Abstract: We investigate the spontaneous scalarization of generic, static, and
spherically symmetric regular black holes supported by nonlinear
electrodynamics. Starting from an arbitrary seed metric, we employ the P-dual
formalism to reconstruct the electromagnetic sector and subsequently couple a
real scalar field nonminimally. As a worked example, we apply the framework to
the regular Balart-Vagenas black hole, showing that scalarized and scalar-free
branches can coexist in a region where the scalarized configurations are
entropically preferred. We further assess possible observational imprints,
finding percent-level deviations in both the shadow size and the fundamental
scalar quasi-normal modes ($< 10\%$ for small charge-to-mass ratios),
indicating that current electromagnetic and gravitational-wave observations do
not rule out these solutions. Our construction thus provides a general route to
explore scalarization on top of nonlinear-electrodynamics-supported spacetimes,
extending beyond specific Reissner-Nordstr\"om-like cases.

</details>


### [128] [Does the survival and sudden death of quadripartite steering in curved spacetime truly depend on multi-directionality?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01561)
*Xiaobao Liu,Wentao Liu,Si-Han Shang,Shu-Min Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究了在史瓦西黑洞背景下高斯四部分量子导引的方向依赖性及其在不同模式间的重新分配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索引力场中量子导引的方向性行为及其在黑洞时空中的演化特性。

Method: 通过分析不同观测者之间的量子导引方向，研究其在霍金温度影响下的动态变化和不对称性。

Result: 发现三种不同行为：非引力到引力方向的导引在最大不对称时突然消失；反向导引单调衰减并在极端黑洞极限下消失；混合分区到非引力模式的导引保持有限渐近值。所有不可达导引均表现出强方向依赖的内在不对称性。

Conclusion: 量子导引具有显著的方向敏感性，其行为受时空曲率和初始压缩参数共同影响，在黑洞环境中呈现丰富的动力学特征。

Abstract: We systematically investigate the directional dependence of Gaussian
quadripartite quantum steering and its redistribution among different modes in
the background of a Schwarzschild black hole. For physically accessible
sectors, we identify three distinct behaviors: (i) steering from
non-gravitational to gravitational observers undergoes sudden death at maximal
asymmetry with the Hawking temperature, marking the crossover from two-way to
one-way steerability; (ii) steering in the opposite direction decays
monotonically and vanishes only in the extreme black hole limit, highlighting
its directional sensitivity to spacetime curvature; (iii) steering from hybrid
gravitational-non-gravitational partitions to non-gravitational mode persists
at a finite asymptotic value set by the initial squeezing parameter. Moreover,
all inaccessible steerings generated by the Hawking effect exhibit an intrinsic
asymmetry, with their specific behavior being strongly dependent on the
steering direction.

</details>


### [129] [Accretion Process as a Probe of Extra Dimensions in MOG Compact Object Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01677)
*Kourosh Nozari,Sara Saghafi,Zeynab Ramezanpasandi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索额外空间维度对引力理论的影响，为统一基本相互作用和量子引力理论提供线索，并解决粒子物理与宇宙学中的开放问题。

Method: 通过解析研究高维、球对称、正则的修正引力致密天体周围的中性粒子动力学及完美流体吸积过程，计算最内稳定圆轨道、能量通量、温度和微分光度等物理量。

Result: 额外维度会减小最内稳定圆轨道半径，同时增强吸积盘的能量通量和温度；通过与Sgr A*的EHT观测数据对比，表明这些修正效应可能接近当前可观测极限。

Abstract: The idea of extra spatial dimensions arises from attempts to unify gravity
with other fundamental interactions, develop a consistent theory of quantum
gravity, and address open problems in particle physics and cosmology.
Considerable attention has been devoted to understanding how such dimensions
modify gravitational theories. One way to probe their impact is through the
analytical study of astrophysical processes such as black hole accretion. Since
accretion efficiently converts gravitational energy into radiation, this makes
it a powerful tool to test modified gravity (MOG) theories and
higher-dimensional frameworks via the behavior of dark compact objects like
black holes, neutron stars, and white dwarfs. In this work, we investigate the
dynamics of neutral particles around a higher-dimensional, regular, spherically
symmetric MOG compact object, focusing on the innermost stable circular orbit
(ISCO), energy flux, temperature, and differential luminosity. We further
analyze the accretion of a perfect fluid onto the same object, deriving
analytical expressions for the four-velocity and proper energy density of the
inflowing matter. Our findings show that extra dimensions reduce the ISCO
radius while enhancing the corresponding flux and temperature. Finally, by
comparing the effective disk temperature $T_{\text{eff}}$ with Event Horizon
Telescope (EHT) observations of Sgr A*, we argue that MOG and
higher-dimensional corrections to the accretion disk properties could be close
to the current threshold of detectability.

### [130] [Semiclassical Gravity Beyond General Relativity: Insights from Torsion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01684)
*R. Morales-Cabrera,Y. Bonder*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发展了具有非平凡时空挠率的修正引力的半经典理论，特别是在四维爱因斯坦-卡当理论中对非最小耦合的自由克莱因-戈登场进行了公理化处理。通过哈达玛重正化，得到了能量-动量和自旋密度算子的良好定义期望值，并分析了在挠率存在下依然存在的共形反常。

Result: 获得了能量-动量和自旋密度算子的明确期望值，揭示了尺度和重正化模糊性，并确认了在存在挠率的情况下共形反常仍然存在。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在包含挠率的修正引力理论中，可以通过适当的重正化方法实现半经典处理，并且共形反常在该背景下依然成立。

Abstract: We develop a semiclassical theory of modified gravity with nontrivial

energy--momentum and spin--density operators. These objects exhibit scale and
renormalization ambiguities; we identify the latter by constructing a
renormalization Lagrangian in terms of differential forms, which are
particularly well suited for this purpose. Furthermore, we analyze the

### [131] [Baryogenesis constraints on generalized mass-to-horizon entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01693)
*Giuseppe Gaetano Luciano,Emmanuel N. Saridakis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于广义质量-视界熵的宇宙学框架下的重子不对称性生成，发现对贝肯斯坦-霍金熵的微小偏离可能与当前宇宙学观测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在修正的熵-面积关系下，如何自然产生重子不对称性，并与当前宇宙学观测保持一致。

Method: 基于广义质量-视界熵，应用引力-热力学猜想，推导修正的弗里德曼方程，并研究其对重子数产生的影响。

Result: 修正的熵导致Hubble参数演化改变，即使标准超引力耦合也能产生非零的物质-反物质不对称性；观测数据限制熵指数满足0 < 1 - n ≲ O(10^{-2})。

Conclusion: 轻微但物理上显著偏离标准贝肯斯坦-霍金熵（n=1）可能是实现与当前宇宙观测完全一致所必需的。

Abstract: We investigate the generation of the baryon asymmetry within the cosmological
framework based on a generalized mass-to-horizon entropy. This entropy,
recently proposed as a power-law extension of the Bekenstein-Hawking area law,
arises from a modified mass-horizon relation constructed to ensure consistency
with the Clausius relation. By applying the gravity-thermodynamics conjecture,
the resulting corrections to the Friedmann equations modify the evolution of
the Hubble parameter. Consequently, even the standard supergravity coupling
between the Ricci scalar and the baryon current can generate a non-vanishing
matter-antimatter asymmetry. Comparison with observational data yields a
stringent constraint on the entropic exponent, namely $0 < 1 - n \lesssim
\mathcal{O}(10^{-2})$, at the decoupling temperature $T_D \simeq
10^{16}\,\text{GeV}$, corresponding to the current upper limit on tensor-mode
fluctuations at the inflationary scale. These findings indicate that minor,
subtle, yet physically significant departures, from the standard
Bekenstein-Hawking entropy ($n = 1$) may be required to achieve full
consistency with present cosmological observations.

### [132] [On energy and its positivity in spacetimes with an expanding flat de Sitter background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01713)
*Rodrigo Avalos,Eric Ling,Annachiara Piubello*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在具有umbilic第二基本形式的膨胀宇宙背景下初始数据集的能量定义，采用de Sitter时空作为背景，并通过调整Liu-Yau能量来定义准局部能量，证明了在某些有界宇宙常数下该能量的正定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于实际天体存在于膨胀的宇宙中而非孤立系统，传统的以Minkowski时空为背景的正能量定理不适用，因此需要建立适用于具有umbilic第二基本形式的宇宙学背景下的能量概念。

Method: 以de Sitter时空为背景，在平坦膨胀坐标下将其分解为一系列等距于欧几里得3-空间的umbilic超曲面，引入准局部能量定义，并借鉴Liu-Yau能量方法进行调整和应用。

Result: 提出了适用于膨胀宇宙背景的准局部能量定义，并证明了在特定有界宇宙常数范围内该能量具有正定性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功推广了正能量定理至包含宇宙膨胀效应的物理场景，为非孤立引力系统的能量描述提供了新的数学框架。

Abstract: The positive energy theorems are a fundamental pillar in mathematical general
relativity. Originally proved by Schoen-Yau and later Witten, these theorems
were established for asymptotically flat manifolds where the metric tends to
the standard Euclidean metric and whose second fundamental form decays to zero
at infinity. This ansatz on the metric and second fundamental form is motivated
by the desire to model an isolated gravitational system with a Minkowski space
background for the spacetime. However, actual astrophysical massive objects are
not truly isolated but rather exist within an expanding cosmological universe,
where the second fundamental form is umbilic. With this in mind, we seek a
notion of energy for initial data sets with an umbilic second fundamental form.
In this work, we present a definition of energy in such an expanding
cosmological setting. Instead of Minkowski space, we take de Sitter space as
the background spacetime, which, when written in flat-expanding coordinates, is
foliated by umbilic hypersurfaces each isometric to Euclidean 3-space. This
cosmological setting necessitates a quasi-local energy definition, as the
presence of a cosmological horizon in de Sitter space obstructs a global one.
We define energy in this quasi-local setting by adapting the Liu-Yau energy to
our framework and establish positivity of this energy for certain bounded
values of the cosmological constant.

</details>

### [133] [Hadronic scattering in (1+1)D SU(2) lattice gauge theory from tensor networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00154)
*João Barata,Juan Hormaza,Zhong-Bo Kang,Wenyang Qian*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 首次基于张量网络技术在(1+1)维SU(2)格点规范理论中实现非阿贝尔实时散射的第一性原理研究，揭示了不同重子数扇区中的弹性与非弹性碰撞行为，特别是在B=1扇区中出现的纠缠与空间离域现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非阿贝尔规范理论中强耦合下实时强子散射的动力学行为，填补第一性原理实时模拟的空白。

Method: 采用无规范场的哈密顿形式化方法，通过张量网络技术精确积出规范场，无需截断电通量，在固定全局重子数B=0,1,2的扇区中研究散射过程。

Result: B=0和B=2扇区主要表现为类似U(1) Schwinger模型的弹性动力学；B=1扇区展现出新奇行为：碰撞中介子与重子波包发生纠缠，慢态空间离域，快态弹道传播，通过局域观测量、纠缠熵和信息晶格刻画相关性演化。

Conclusion: 该工作为非阿贝尔规范理论中的实时散射提供了首个第一性原理基准，并为量子模拟重子数动力学和非弹性过程开辟了道路。

Abstract: We present a first real-time study of hadronic scattering in a
(1+1)-dimensional SU(2) lattice gauge theory with fundamental fermions using
tensor-network techniques. Working in the gaugeless Hamiltonian formulation --
where the gauge field is exactly integrated out and no truncation of the
electric flux is required -- we investigate scattering processes across sectors
of fixed global baryon number $B = 0, 1, 2$. These correspond respectively to
meson--meson, meson--baryon, and baryon--baryon collisions. At strong coupling,
the $B = 0$ and $B = 2$ channels exhibit predominantly elastic dynamics closely
resembling those of the U(1) Schwinger model. In contrast, the mixed $B = 1$
sector shows qualitatively new behavior: meson and baryon wave packets become
entangled during the collision, and depending on their initial kinematics, the
slower state becomes spatially delocalized while the faster one propagates
ballistically. We characterize these processes through local observables,
entanglement entropy, and the information-lattice, which together reveal how
correlations build up and relax during the interaction. Our results establish a
first benchmark for non-Abelian real-time scattering from first principles and
open the path toward quantum-simulation studies of baryon-number dynamics and
inelastic processes in gauge theories.

</details>


### [134] [opbasis - a Python package to derive minimal operator bases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00165)
*Nikolai Husung*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个针对格点场论中有效场论（EFT）研究的Python工具包，用于构建满足特定对称性（如离散超立方对称性）的算符基底，解决了传统连续场论方法在格点情境下的瓶颈问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在格点有效场论中，构造满足离散对称性的完备且极小的算符基底是系统研究领头阶对数修正和格点误差的关键步骤，但现有连续场论工具难以直接应用。

Method: 开发了一个灵活的Python软件包，支持用户自定义对称性、扭曲质量、洛伦兹提升等扩展功能，并通过三个逐步复杂的实例展示其用法：Wilson QCD中轴矢量的O(a)算符基、未根Staggered夸克对称性下的算符基，以及具有赝标量量子数的B*π算符构造。

Result: 该工具包成功实现了针对4维非阿贝尔格点规范理论的有效场论算符基构造，并展示了其在不同对称性和物理场景下的可扩展性与实用性。

Conclusion: 该Python包为格点场论研究者提供了一个高效、灵活的工具，能够自动化生成满足复杂离散对称性的算符基底，显著提升了有效场论分析的效率，并具备向更广泛理论场景拓展的潜力。

Abstract: Finding a complete and yet minimal on-shell basis of operators of a given
mass-dimension that are compatible with a specific set of transformation
properties is the first step in any Effective Field Theory description. This
step is the main bottleneck for systematic studies of leading logarithmic
corrections to integer-power lattice artifacts in Symanzik Effective Field
Theory targeting various local fields and lattice actions. The focus on
discrete symmetry transformations in lattice field theory, especially reduced
hypercubic spacetime symmetry with Euclidean signature, complicates the use of
standard continuum field theory tools.
  Here, a new Python package is being presented that targets the typical
lattice field-theorist's use cases. While the main target lies on continuum
EFTs describing 4D non-Abelian lattice gauge theories, the applicability can be
extended beyond Effective Field Theories. New discrete symmetries, twisted
masses, or the introduction of boosts are just a few examples of possible
extensions that can be easily implemented by the user. This should allow for a
wider range of theories and applications beyond the initial focus of this
package.
  The general functionality of the package is explained along the lines of
three examples: The $\mathrm{O}(a)$ operator basis of the axial-vector in
Wilson QCD, operator bases compatible with the symmetries of unrooted Staggered
quarks as well as a pedestrian derivation of a
$B^*(\mathbf{p})\pi(-\mathbf{p})$ operator with pseudo-scalar quantum numbers.
Each example makes use of an increasing range of features and requires
user-defined extensions show-casing the versatility of the package.

</details>


### [135] [An effective field theory for thermal QCD with 2+1 flavours](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00409)
*Sourendu Gupta,Pritam Sen,Rishi Sharma*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文构建了QCD在有限温度下略低于相变温度$T_c$的长距离有效场论（EFT），并利用格点QCD数据拟合其低能常数，成功预测了静态介子性质、相图、压强及动能质量等物理量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在QCD相变附近构建有效的低能理论，以连接格点模拟结果与实际物理观测量，并外推预测尚未测量的物理量。

Method: 基于手征有效理论框架，结合两个温度下的格点QCD测量数据（介子屏蔽质量）拟合低能常数，进而用于预测其他静态和动态物理量。

Result: 该EFT对$N_f=2$情形下的静态介子性质给出良好预测；成功描述$N_f=2+1$的相图；并对压强和实时间维克转动后的动能质量作出可检验的预测。

Conclusion: 所构建的有效场论能够准确刻画QCD在接近相变区的长距离行为，是连接格点数据与物理预测的有力工具。

Abstract: We write a long-distance effective field theory (EFT) for QCD at finite
temperature just below the crossover temperature $T_c$. The low energy
constants (LECs) of this EFT are obtained from lattice measurements of the
screening mass of pions at two temperatures for $N_f=2+1$ using lattice results
obtained at physical values of pion and Kaon masses, and $N_f=2$ where the
lattice simulations were performed with a heavier pion mass. The EFT gives good
predictions for other static pion properties for $N_f=2$, where lattice results
are available. We show the corresponding predictions for $N_f=2+1$, where they
are not yet measured. We demonstrate that EFT gives excellent predictions for
the phase diagram in $N_f=2+1$. The predictions for the pressure are
investigated, and predictions are also given for a Wick-rotated real-time
quantity called the kinetic mass.

</details>


### [136] [Precision lattice calculation of the hadronic contribution to the running of the electroweak gauge couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01623)
*Alessandro Conigli,Dalibor Djukanovic,Georg von Hippel,Simon Kuberski,Harvey B. Meyer,Kohtaroh Miura,Konstantin Ottnad,Andreas Risch,Hartmut Wittig*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过格点QCD计算了电磁耦合跑动的强子贡献及电弱混合角，在多体系统和物理π质量下实现了高精度结果，发现与e+e−数据驱动方法存在显著偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确计算强子对电磁耦合跑动和电弱混合角的影响，检验标准模型预测并与实验数据对比。

Method: 基于CLS组态的Nf=2+1味O(a)改进Wilson费米子，采用望远镜窗策略分离系统误差，并结合低模平均与谱重构提升统计精度。

Result: 在Q^2=1 GeV^2处与e+e−数据驱动结果存在高达7σ偏差；在Z极点得到Δα_had^(5)(M_Z^2)=0.027813(33)_lat(35)_pQCD，精度超过现有数据驱动结果两倍以上；对电弱混合角的八重-单态混合分量也给出高精度确定。

Conclusion: 格点QCD可提供比实验数据驱动方法更精确的强子贡献计算，当前结果略偏离全局电弱拟合，可能暗示需重新审视相关理论或实验输入。

Abstract: We present an update of our lattice QCD determination of the hadronic
contribution to the running of the electromagnetic coupling,
$\Delta\alpha_{\mathrm{had}}^{(5)}(-Q^2)$, and of the electroweak mixing angle
in the space-like momentum region up to $Q^2=12\ \mathrm{GeV}^2$. The
calculation is based on CLS ensembles with $N_f=2+1$ flavours of
$O(a)$-improved Wilson fermions, covering five lattice spacings between $0.039$
and $0.085$ fm and a range of pion masses, including the physical point. A
refined analysis employing a telescopic window strategy allows for a clean
separation of systematic effects across Euclidean distance scales. Statistical
precision is further enhanced through low-mode averaging, combined with a
spectral reconstruction of the vector-vector correlator at long distances on
the most chiral ensembles. We confirm significant tensions of up to $7\sigma$
at space-like virtualities around $Q^2= 1\ \mathrm{GeV}^2$ between our lattice
results for $\Delta\alpha_{\mathrm{had}}^{(5)}(-Q^2)$ and the corresponding
data-driven estimates based on $e^+e^-$ cross section data. Combining our
lattice data with perturbative QCD via the Euclidean split technique, we obtain
at the $Z$-pole $\Delta\alpha_{\mathrm{had}}^{(5)}(M_Z^2) =
0.027813(33)_{\mathrm{lat}}(35)_{\mathrm{pQCD}}$, which is more than two times
more precise than recent data-driven estimates. Our result deviates slightly,
by $1-2\sigma$, from the value produced by global electroweak fits. For the
electroweak mixing angle, we present the hadronic contribution to its running
and provide a precise determination of the octet-singlet mixing component
$\bar\Pi^{(0,8)}$, in good agreement with phenomenological models but with
significantly higher precision.

</details>


### [137] [Skewness-dependent Moments of Pion GPD from Nonlocal Quark-Bilinear Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01818)
*Xiang Gao,Swagato Mukherjee,Qi Shi,Fei Yao,Yong Zhao*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过格点QCD计算了π介子价夸克广义部分子分布（GPD）的奇数阶Mellin矩，最高至五阶⟨x⁴⟩，并在[-0.33, 0]的偏斜范围内使用双局域夸克双线性算符的算符乘积展开。计算基于格距a=0.04 fm、价π介子质量300 MeV的组态，并采用动量高达2.428 GeV的加速π介子态，动量转移达2.748 GeV²。研究使用比值方案重整化和次领对数精度的微扰匹配。在零偏斜时结果与先前格点研究一致，并通过多项式约束拟合获得偏斜依赖的矩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确理解π介子内部结构及其广义部分子分布（GPD）的矩信息，特别是在非零偏斜条件下的行为，对强相互作用和核物理具有重要意义。现有格点QCD研究在高阶矩和偏斜依赖性方面仍有限，需更精确计算以支持实验和理论发展。

Method: 采用格点QCD方法，在细密格点（a=0.04 fm）上使用300 MeV价π介子质量的组态，利用加速π介子态提取不同偏斜和动量转移下的矩阵元；通过算符乘积展开关联GPD矩，并应用比值方案进行重整化及次领对数微扰匹配；结合多个偏斜和动量转移数据，进行多项式性约束的全局拟合以提取偏斜依赖的矩。

Result: 成功计算出GPD的奇数阶Mellin矩直至⟨x⁴⟩，覆盖偏斜范围[-0.33, 0]；在零偏斜下结果与先前格点研究一致；通过多点联合拟合，首次在该设置下获得偏斜依赖的高阶矩；动量转移达到2.748 GeV²，为当前较高精度计算之一。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，通过精细格点计算结合高动量态与先进拟合方法，可有效提取GPD的高阶偏斜矩，验证了格点QCD在研究强子内部结构中的可靠性，并为未来实验如深度虚康普顿散射提供重要理论输入。

Abstract: We present lattice QCD calculations of the odd Mellin moments of pion
valence-quark generalized parton distribution (GPD) up to fifth order, $\langle
x^4\rangle$, and for the skewness range $[-0.33, 0]$ using operator product
expansion of bilocal quark-bilinear operators. The calculations are performed
on an ensemble with lattice spacing $a=0.04~\mathrm{fm}$ and valence pion mass
$300$ $\mathrm{MeV}$, employing boosted pion states with momenta up to 2.428
GeV and momentum transfers reaching 2.748 GeV$^2$. We employ ratio-scheme
renormalization and next-to-leading-logarithmic resummed perturbative matching.
At zero skewness, our results are consistent with previous lattice studies. By
combining matrix elements at multiple values of skewness and momentum transfer,
skewness-dependent moments are obtained through simultaneous
polynomiality-constrained fits.

</details>
